ɓasendulo ezitʰeni zetʰu nasesanɮeni saɓo ɓoŋke aɓasizondajo okʰokʰo ɓetʰu nokukʰumbula sajo esiŋǀ̤wele isifuŋo ejasifuŋa kuɓaɓa uaɓrahama ukuɓa sitʰi sikʰululiwe esanɮeni sezitʰa zetʰu sijikʰonze siŋenakwesaɓa ŋoɓuŋǀ̤wele naŋokuluŋa pʰambi kwajo zoŋke zetʰu naweke ujakutʰiwa umprofetʰi wopʰezukoŋke ŋokuɓa ujakuhamba pʰambi kweŋkosi ukuluŋisa izinɮela zajo aɓantu ɓajo ukujazi ŋokutʰetʰelelwa zaɓo ŋemisesane jesihawu sikaŋkuluŋkulu wetʰu esizakuhaɲd͡ʒelwa ŋajo ŋukusa kwapʰezulu ukuɓakʰaɲisela aɓaɬezi eɓumɲameni nasetʰunzini nokuǃondisa iziɲawo zetʰu enɮeleni jokutʰula wakʰulake waɓa namanɮa emojeni waɬala eɬane kwaɓa lokuɓonakaliswa kwakʰe kuisrajeli kwatʰi ŋalezo kwapʰuma kukesari awuɡustu sokuɓa kuɓalwe loŋke lokʰu kuɓalwa kokuǃala ukʰureniju eŋumbusi wasesirija ɓoŋke ɓaja kuɓalwa jilowo wakuɓo naje ud͡ʒosefa wakʰupʰuka epʰuma eɡalile wasenazaretʰa waja ed͡ʒudija kadavide otʰiwa iɓetlehema ŋokuɓa wajeŋowenɮu lukadavide ukujoɓalwa kaɲe nomarija owajemmiselwe ukuɓa aɓe ŋumkakʰe ekʰulelwe kwatʰike ɓeselapʰo zapʰelela zokuɓa aɓeletʰe waziɓula ŋendodana wajembesa wajilalisa emkʰombeni ŋokuɓa ɓantula enɮini jezihambi kwakukʰona aɓelusi aɓaɓeɬezi enɮe ɓelinda umɬambi waɓo eɓusuku iŋelosi jeŋkosi jema pʰambi kwaɓo iŋkazimulo jeŋkosi jaɓakʰaɲisa ŋǁazoŋke ɓesaɓa ŋokwesaɓa okukʰulu iŋelosi jatʰi kuɓo niŋesaɓi ŋokuɓa bekani ŋiniɓikela izindaɓa ezinɬe zokutʰokoza okukʰulu okuzakuɓa kuɓantu ɓoŋke ukutʰi namuɬa umsindisi oŋukristu iŋkosi kadavide nalokʰu kujisiɓoniso nijakufumana emkʰombeni masiɲane kwaɓa kʰona kaɲe neŋelosi uǃuǃaɓa lweɓanɮa uŋkuluŋkulu lutʰi udumo kuŋkuluŋkulu kwelipʰezulu nokutʰula emɬaɓeni kuɓantu aɓatʰokozelwa ŋuje kwatʰi ukuɓa kuɓo iziŋelosi zija aɓelusi ɓakʰuluma ɓodwa ɓatʰi asihambe maɲd͡ʒe eɓetlehema siɓone lejo ejenzekilejo iŋkosi jona ɓepʰutʰuma ɓafika ɓafumanisa omarija nod͡ʒosefa emkʰombeni seɓeɓonile ɓalanda ŋalelo aɓaɓet͡ʃelwe ŋalowo ɓoŋke aɓezwajo ɓamaŋala ŋokukʰuluɲwe kuɓo ŋaɓelusi kepʰa umarija waɡǀ̤ina oŋke ezinɮa ŋawo enɬizijweni jakʰe ɓaɓujake aɓelusi ɓemdumisa ɓemboŋa uŋkuluŋkulu ŋakʰo koŋke aɓakuzwilejo naɓakuɓonilejo ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰo kwakukʰuluɲiwe kuɓo kwatʰi sezipʰelile ezijisiʃijaɡalombili zokuɓa iɡama lakʰe latʰiwa ud͡ʒesu elaliǃaɲd͡ʒiwe jiŋelosi eŋakatʰat͡ʃatʰwa kwatʰi ukuɓa kupʰelele zokuɬaɲd͡ʒululwa kwaɓo ŋokomtʰetʰo kamose ɓeɲukela naje ed͡ʒerusalema ukuɓa ɓammise pʰambi kweŋkosi ɲd͡ʒeŋokulot͡ʃiwe emtʰetʰweni weŋkosi ukutʰi koŋke okujiziɓulo kujakutʰiwa okwaɬukaniselwe iŋkosi ɓanikele ŋomɬat͡ʃelo ɲd͡ʒeŋokuʃiwo emtʰetʰweni weŋkosi amahobe amaɓili amapʰupʰu amaɓili amad͡ʒuɓa beka kwakukʰona ed͡ʒerusalema oɡama lakʰe liŋusimejoni wajeluŋile emesaɓa uŋkuluŋkulu ebekile kaisrajeli nomoja oŋǀ̤wele wajepʰezu kwakʰe kwakuɓonakalisiwe kuje ŋomoja oŋǀ̤wele ukutʰi akajikuɓona eŋakamboni ukristu weŋkosi wafika ŋomoja etʰempelini kwatʰi ukuɓa aɓazali ɓaletʰe ud͡ʒesu etʰempelini ukuɓa ɓenze kuje ɲd͡ʒeŋesiko lomtʰetʰo ŋokumɡona wamboŋa uŋkuluŋkulu watʰi sale ŋokutʰula iŋǀeku jakʰo somanɮa ɲd͡ʒeŋezwi lakʰo ŋokuɓa ameɬo aɓonile jakʰo ojiluŋisele eɓusweni ɓaɓantu ɓoŋke ukukʰaɲa aɓezizwe neŋkazimulo jesizwe sakʰo uisrajeli ujise ɓamaŋala ŋalokʰo okukʰuluɲwa ŋaje usimejoni waɓaɓusisa watʰi kumarija beka kwaɓaniŋi kuisrajeli nesiɓonakaliso esipʰikwajo jeɓo iŋkemba ijakudaɓula nowakʰo umpʰefumulo ukuɓa izizinɮo zezinɬizijo eziniŋi kwakukʰona nomprofetʰikazi uana kafanuweli sikaaseri wajesekʰulile kakʰulu eɓeɬalile imiɲaka ejisikʰombisa koɓuntombi ɓakʰe eŋumfelokazi waɓa nemiɲaka eŋamaʃumi ajisiʃijaɡalombili eŋasuki etʰempelini ekʰonza ŋokuzila naŋokukʰuleka uɓusuku najeke ŋasona sikʰatʰi uŋkuluŋkulu wakʰuluma ŋaje kuɓo ɓoŋke aɓaɓebeke ukukʰululwa kwed͡ʒerusalema kwatʰi seɓefeze koŋke okuŋokomtʰetʰo weŋkosi ɓaɓujela eɡalile wakuɓo inazaretʰa wakʰula waɓa namanɮa waɡǀ̤wala ukuɬakanipʰa kaŋkuluŋkulu wawupʰezu kwakʰe aɓazali ɓakʰe ɓaja ed͡ʒerusalema imiɲaka joŋke ŋomkʰosi wepʰasika esenemiɲaka ejiʃumi ɓakʰupʰuka ɲd͡ʒeŋokomtʰetʰo womkʰosi seɓeziǃedile ekuɓujeni kwaɓo ud͡ʒesu ed͡ʒerusalema aɓazali ɓakʰe ɓeŋazi ɓetʰike ɓona upʰakatʰi kwaɓahambisana naɓo ɓahamba iɓaŋa ɓamfuna pʰakatʰi kweziɬoɓo naɓazana naɓo ɓeŋamtʰoli ɓaɓujela ed͡ʒerusalema ɓemfuna kwatʰi ezintatʰu ɓamfumana etʰempelini eɬezi pʰakatʰi kwaɓafundisi eɓezwa eɓaɓuza ɓoŋke aɓaɓemuzwa ɓamaŋala ŋokuǃonda naŋokupʰendula kwakʰe ɓatʰi ɓembona ɓamaŋala watʰi kuje mntanami okuɲd͡ʒe beka ujiɬo ɓesikufuna watʰi kuɓo kukaɲd͡ʒani ɓeniŋifunelani ɓeniŋazi jini ukutʰi ukuɓa ŋiɓe kokukaɓaɓa aɓaliǃondaŋa aɓelikʰuluma kuɓo weɬa naɓo enazaretʰa waɓatʰoɓela kepʰa wawaɡǀ̤ina oŋke enɬizijweni jakʰe ud͡ʒesu waǃʰuɓeka ekuɬakanipʰeni nasekukʰuleni kuŋkuluŋkulu nakuɓantu kwatʰi ŋomɲaka weʃumi nanɬanu wokuɓusa kukatiɓeriju kesari upontiju pilatu eŋumbusi wased͡ʒudija uherode eŋumtetrarki waseɡalile ufilipʰu umfowaɓo eŋumtetrarki laseitureja nelasetrakʰoniti ulisanija eŋumtetrarki waseaɓilene uanase eŋumpristi omkʰulu nokajafase likaŋkuluŋkulu kud͡ʒohane kazakarija eɬane weza loŋke lased͡ʒordani eʃumajela umbhapatʰizo wokupʰenduka kuɓe ŋukutʰetʰelelwa ɲd͡ʒeŋokuɓa kulot͡ʃiwe eŋǀwadini jamazwi kaisaja umprofetʰi ukutʰi izwi lomemezajo eɬane litʰi ‘luŋisani inɮela jeŋkosi imikʰondo jajo iǃonde iziɡodi zoŋke zijakuɡǃ̤it͡ʃwa zoŋke izintaɓa namaɡǃ̤uma kujakweɬiswa kuǃonde izinsoŋansoŋa nemiɡoǁiɡoǁi iɓe jizinɮela iɲama joŋke izakuɓona kaŋkuluŋkulu ŋakʰoke watʰi eziǁukwini ezazipʰumela ukubapatʰizwa ŋuje nzalo jeziɲoka uɓani oniɓonise ukuɓalekela intukutʰelo ezajo ŋakʰo izitʰelo ukupʰenduka niŋaǃali ukutʰi pʰakatʰi ‘sinoɓaɓa uaɓrahama ŋokuɓa ŋitʰi uŋkuluŋkulu unamanɮa uaɓrahama aɓantwana mat͡ʃe namaɲd͡ʒe seliɓekiwe jemitʰi ŋakʰo joŋke imitʰi eŋatʰeli isitʰelo esiɬe ijaŋǃuɲwa ipʰonswe iziǁuku zatʰi pʰo wapʰendula watʰi kuɓo oneziŋuɓo akamupʰe oŋenajo naje onokuɮa ɲd͡ʒalo kwafika naɓatʰelisi ukuɓa ɓabapatʰizwe ɓatʰi kuje mfundisi watʰi kuɓo niŋaɓizi lutʰo ŋapʰezu kwenikumiselwejo namaɓutʰo atʰi tʰinake watʰi niŋamuki lutʰo ŋenɮuzula niŋamǁabeleli janeliswani jiziŋkokʰelo aɓantu ɓesabekile ɓezinɮa ɓoŋke ezinɬizijweni zaɓo ŋod͡ʒohane ukutʰi iŋaɓe uŋukristu jini ud͡ʒohane wapʰendula watʰi kuɓo ɓoŋke mina ŋinibapatʰiza ŋamanzi kepʰa ujeza onamanɮa eŋiŋafanele ukutʰukulula umǀʰilo weziǀatʰulo zakʰe jena uzakunibapatʰiza ŋomoja oŋǀ̤wele naŋomlilo oǃoma lakʰe lisesanɮeni sakʰe ukuʃanelisisa isiɓuja sakʰe nokuɓutʰela eŋǃoloɓaneni jakʰe kepʰa amakʰoɓa uzakuwaʃisa ŋomlilo oŋaǀimekijo naŋokuɲe okuniŋi waʃumajela ivaŋeli kuɓantu eɓajala kepʰa uherode ŋuje ŋeŋǁa kaherodija umkamfowaɓo naŋeŋǁa jakʰo koŋke okuɓi aɓekwenzile uherode nalokʰu kokuɲe koŋke ud͡ʒohane etiloŋweni kwatʰi ɓebapatʰiziwe aɓantu ɓoŋke naje ud͡ʒesu esebapatʰiziwe ekʰuleka umoja oŋǀ̤wele ɲd͡ʒeŋed͡ʒuɓa weɬela pʰezu kwakʰe litʰi wena ujindodana jami etʰandekajo ŋitʰokozile ŋawe jena ud͡ʒesu ukuǃala kwakʰe wajenemiɲaka eŋaɓa ŋamaʃumi amatʰatʰu ejindodana ɲd͡ʒeŋokuʃiwojo kad͡ʒosefa kaeli kamatʰati kalevi kameliki kad͡ʒanaji kad͡ʒosefa kamatatʰija kaamose kanahume kaeseli kanaɡaji kamati kamatatʰija kasemejini kad͡ʒosefa kad͡ʒuda kad͡ʒohanani karesa kazoroɓaɓeli kasalatijeli kaneri kameliki kaadi kakosamu kaelimadamu kaeri kad͡ʒose kaelijezeri kad͡ʒorimi kamatʰati kalevi kasimejoni kad͡ʒuda kad͡ʒosefa kad͡ʒonamu kaelijakimi kameleja kamena kamatʰata kanatʰamu kadavide kad͡ʒesaji kaoɓede kaɓowasi kasala kanasoni kaaminadaɓa kaadamejini kaarani kaesiromu kafaresi kad͡ʒuda kad͡ʒakoɓe kaisaka kaaɓraɓama katʰara kanahori kaseruki karaɡawu kafaleki kaeɓere kasala kakajinamu kaarfakisadi kasemi kanowa kalameka kamatʰusala kaenoke kad͡ʒaretʰi kamalelejeli kakajinani kaenose kaseti kaadamu kaŋkuluŋkulu ud͡ʒesu eɡǀ̤wele umoja oŋǀ̤wele waɓuja ed͡ʒordani ŋomoja eɬane eliŋwa ŋusatʰane eziŋamaʃumi akaɮaŋa lutʰo sezipʰelile wajesetʰi kuje usatʰane uma ujindodana kaŋkuluŋkulu jiʃo t͡ʃe ukuɓa liɓe jisiŋkwa ud͡ʒesu wampʰendula watʰi kulot͡ʃiwe ukutʰi ‘akusiŋkwa azakupʰila ŋaso esemeɲusela entaɓeni imiɓuso joŋke jezwe ŋomzuzwaɲana usatʰane watʰi kuje amanɮa oŋke ŋokunika kaɲe neŋkazimulo jawo ŋokuɓa futʰi ŋijinika uɓani ŋokutʰanda ŋakʰoke ukʰuleka pʰambi koŋke kuzakuɓa ŋokwakʰo ud͡ʒesu wapʰendula watʰi kuje kulot͡ʃiwe ukutʰi ‘wokʰuleka eŋkosini uŋkuluŋkulu wakʰo umkʰonze jena jedwa wajesemholela ed͡ʒerusalema esiǃoŋweni setʰempeli watʰi kuje uma ujindodana kaŋkuluŋkulu zipʰonse pʰansi lapʰa ŋokuɓa kulot͡ʃiwe ukutʰi ‘ujakujaleza iziŋelosi zakʰe ŋawe nokutʰi ‘zijakukutʰwala ŋezanɮa uŋaze waǃʰuzuka et͡ʃeni ŋoɲawo lwakʰo ud͡ʒesu wapʰendula watʰi kuje kwatʰiwa ‘uŋajiliŋi iŋkosi uŋkuluŋkulu wakʰo usatʰane eseǃede ukuliŋa koŋke kuje isikʰatʰi ud͡ʒesu waɓujela eɡalile ŋamanɮa kamoja lwakʰe loŋke laŋakʰona wafundisa emasinaɡoɡeni aɓo eduɲiswa jiɓo ɓoŋke wafika enazaretʰa lapʰo wajonɮiwa kʰona waŋena esinaɡoɡeni ŋosuku lwesaɓatʰa ɲd͡ʒeŋokwenza kwakʰe wanikwa iŋǀwadi kaisaja umprofetʰi wajivula iŋǀwadi okulot͡ʃwe kujo ukutʰi umoja weŋkosi upʰezu ŋokuɓa iŋiɡǀ̤oɓile ukuɓa ŋiʃumajele ivaŋeli kwaɓampofu iŋitʰumele ukukʰululwa kwaɓatʰuɲd͡ʒiwejo nokuɓona kwaɓajizimpumputʰe nokuɬeŋa aɓaǀindezelwejo umɲaka omuɬe weŋkosi wajiɡoǃoŋa iŋǀwadi wajinika isikʰonzi waɬala ameɬo aɓo ɓoŋke aɓaɓesesinaɡoɡeni amɡǃ̤olozela waǃala ukukʰuluma kuɓo etʰi namɬaɲd͡ʒe uɡǀ̤walisekile ezinɮeɓeni ɓoŋke ɓamfakazela ɓemaŋala ŋamazwi apʰuma emloɲeni wakʰe ɓatʰi lo akasijo kad͡ʒosefa watʰi kuɓo nempela nijakuʃo saɡa sokutʰi ‘ɲaŋa zelapʰe lokʰo ekapernawume nalapʰa watʰike ŋiǃinisile ŋitʰi akukʰo mprofetʰi lakuɓo kepʰa ŋempela ŋitʰi kwakukʰona kwaisrajeli aɓafelokazi aɓaniŋi emiɬeni kaelija lapʰo imiɲaka emitʰatʰu neziɲaŋa ezijisitʰupʰa kwaɓa kʰona inɮala eŋkulu loŋke kepʰa uelija katʰuɲelwaŋa nakojedwa kuɓona kupʰela esarepita lasesidoni oŋumfelokazi kwakukʰona futʰi kwaisrajeli aɓanoǀʰoko aɓaniŋi ŋesikʰatʰi sikaeliʃa umprofetʰi kepʰa akuɬaɲd͡ʒululwaŋa namuɲe kuɓo kupʰela unajimani umsirija ɓoŋke aɓaɓesesinaɡoɡeni ɓaɡǀ̤wala ɓekuzwa lokʰo ɓasukuma ɓamǁoʃa ɓamǃʰuɓela ekweŋameni kwentaɓa waɓo owakʰiwe pʰezu kwajo ɓamkʰalakatʰelisele pʰansi kepʰa jena edaɓula pʰakatʰi kwaɓo weɬela ekapernawume waseɡalile wajeɓafundisa ŋosuku lwesaɓatʰa ɓamaŋala ŋokufundisa kwakʰe ŋokuɓa lakʰe lalinamanɮa kwakukʰona esinaɡoɡeni onomoja eliŋǀ̤olilejo ŋezwi elikʰulu watʰi ɦija sinamseɓenzi d͡ʒesu wasenazaretʰa uze ukusibubisa ŋijakwazi ukuɓa uŋuɓani uŋoŋǀ̤wele kaŋkuluŋkulu ud͡ʒesu wamkʰuza watʰi tʰula upʰume kuje idemoni lampʰonsa pʰansi pʰakatʰi kwaɓo lapʰuma kuje liŋamlimazaŋa ɓeɬelwa ŋukwesaɓa ɓoŋke ɓakʰuluma ɓodwa ɓatʰi jizwi lokuɓa ajale omoja aɓaŋǀ̤olilejo ŋeɡuɲa naŋamanɮa ɓapʰume kwanda ŋaje zoŋke zaŋakʰona wasuka esinaɡoɡeni waŋena enɮini kasimoni kepʰa umkʰwekazi kasimoni wajeɓaɲd͡ʒwe ŋumkʰuɬane omkʰulu ɓamŋǁusa ŋaje wameŋama wakʰuza umkʰuɬane wamjeka masiɲane waɓakʰonza ukuʃona kwelaŋa ɓoŋke aɓaɓe naɓaɡulajo ŋezifo ɓaɓaletʰa kuje eɓeka izanɮa pʰezu kwaɓo ŋaɓaɲe waɓapʰulukisa kwapʰuma kwaɓaniŋi etʰi wena ujindodana kaŋkuluŋkulu kepʰa wawakʰuza kawavumelaŋa ukuɓa akʰulume ŋokuɓa ajemazi ukutʰi uŋukristu sekusile wapʰuma waja ejiɬane iziǁuku kuje ukuɓa aŋamuki kepʰa watʰi nakwemiɲe ŋimelwe ukuʃumajela ivaŋeli kaŋkuluŋkulu ŋokuɓa ŋitʰuɲelwe lokʰo waʃumajela emasinaɡoɡeni aseɡalile kwatʰi isiǁuku simbuŋaɲela ukuɓa likaŋkuluŋkulu wajemi ŋaselwanɮe lwaseɡenesaretʰa waɓona imikʰumbi emiɓili ŋaselwanɮe aɓadoɓi ɓaɓepʰumile kujo ɓeɬanza amanetʰa eseŋene komuɲe wemikʰumbi oŋokasimoni wamǀela ukuɓa kaŋǀane emɬaɓatʰini waɬala pʰansi waɓafundisa aɓantu esemkʰuɲd͡ʒini kutʰe eseɡǀ̤inile ukukʰuluma watʰi kusimoni ǃʰuɓekela ekud͡ʒuleni neɬise amanetʰa niɓambe usimoni wapʰendula watʰi ŋkosi siʃikile uɓusuku ɓoŋke asiɓambaŋa lutʰo kepʰa ŋezwi lakʰo ŋijakuweɬisa amanetʰa seɓekwenzile lokʰo ɓaɓamba izinɬanzi eziniŋi kakʰulu aɡǃ̤aɓuka amanetʰa aɓo ɓaɓaǃʰweɓa ɓaɓo aɓakomuɲe umkʰumbi ukuɓa ɓeze ɓaɓaɓambise ɓezake ɓajiɡǀ̤walisa imikʰumbi amaɓili ŋokuɓa kokuɲe ijakuzonda eɲe itʰande eɲe iɓambelele kweɲe ijejise eɲe niŋeze nakʰonza uŋkuluŋkulu nomamona aɓafarisi aɓaɓetʰanda ɓakuzwa koŋke lokʰo ɓamkxolodela wajesetʰi kuɓo nina sikʰatʰi ivaŋeli kaŋkuluŋkulu lijaʃuɲajelwa woŋke upʰika ŋokufuzula kepʰa ukuɓa kuɮule nomɬaɓa kunokuɓa iɓalana lomtʰetʰo jilowo olaɬa umkakʰe aɡanwe ŋomuɲe ujapʰiŋa noɡanwa ŋolaɬiwe jindoda ujapʰiŋa kwakukʰona otʰile onotʰilejo owajeɡǃ̤oka eziɓuɓende eliɬe ezid͡ʒaɓulisa imiɬa ŋemiɬa kwakukʰona futʰi otʰile ŋulazaru iɡama lakʰe owajelaɬiwe ŋasesaŋweni lakʰe eɡǀ̤wele eŋǁanela ukusutʰiswa ŋemvutʰuluka lesiǀeɓi jeɓo neziɲd͡ʒa zamkʰotʰa kwase kutʰi watʰwalwa jiziŋelosi esifuɓeni sikaaɓrahama nesiǀeɓi sesisehajidese sapʰakamisa ameɬo siseɓuɬuŋwini uaɓrahama nolazaru esesifuɓeni sakʰe samemeza satʰi ‘ɓaɓa aɓrahama ŋihawukele utʰume ulazaru aɡǀ̤oboze isiɬoko wakʰe apʰozise ŋokuɓa ŋijaɬuʃwa laŋaɓi kepʰa uaɓrahama watʰi ‘ndodana kʰumbula ukuɓa okuɬe kwakʰo usesekupʰileni nolazaru kaɲd͡ʒalo okuɓi maɲd͡ʒe ujaduduzwa jena lapʰa ujaɬuʃwa naŋapʰezu kwakʰo koŋke lokʰo kuɓekiwe umhoʃa omkʰulu pʰakatʰi kwetʰu ukuɓa aɓafuna lapʰa ɓaje ɓaŋekwenze naɓalapʰo ɓaŋaweleli kitʰi sase sitʰi ‘ɲd͡ʒalo ŋijakuǀela ɓaɓa ukuɓa umtʰumele enɮini kaɓaɓa ŋokuɓa ŋinaɓafowetʰu aɓajisiɬanu kuɓo ɓaŋezi naɓo joɓuɬuŋu kepʰa uaɓrahama watʰi ‘ɓanomose naɓaprofetʰi maɓezwe ɓona satʰike ‘ǃʰa ɓaɓa aɓrahama kwaɓafilejo aje kuɓo ɓajakupʰenduka kepʰa watʰi ‘uma ɓeŋalaleli umose naɓaprofetʰi kaɓajikuvuɲiswa kwaɓafilejo wajesetʰi kuɓafundi ɓakʰe kuŋeze ukuɓa kuŋaveli izikʰuɓekiso maje ŋaje kuŋǀ̤ono kuje ukuɓa it͡ʃe liɡaǁwe entaɲeni jakʰe alaɬwe elwanɮe kunokuɓa akʰuɓekise aɓe muɲe kulaɓa aɓaŋǀiɲane ǁwajani uma mkʰuze epʰenduka mtʰetʰelele noma kasikʰombisa ŋosuku aɓujele kasikʰombisa etʰi ‘ŋijapʰenduka womtʰetʰelela aɓapʰostoli ɓase ɓetʰi eŋkosini jandisa ukukʰolwa kwetʰu jajisitʰi iŋkosi uma ɓeninokukʰolwa okuŋaŋenɬamvu jesinapʰi ɓeniŋaʃo mtʰombe ‘simbuka ut͡ʃaleke elwanɮe uɓujakunilalela ŋumupʰi oneŋǀeku elimajo nokuɓa ejalusajo atʰi kujo iɓuja enɮe ‘sondela masiɲane uɬale pʰansi uɮe kodwa akajikuʃo kujo ukutʰi ‘luŋisa eŋizakukuɮa uziɓopʰe uŋipʰakele ŋize ŋiɮe ŋipʰuze andukuɓa uɮe upʰuze ujajiɓoŋa jini iŋǀeku ŋokuɓa jenzile ekujaliwejo kuɲd͡ʒalo ŋǁa koŋke enikujaliwejo anotʰi ‘asiziŋǀeku zalutʰo ɲd͡ʒe eɓesifanele kwatʰi ukuja ed͡ʒerusalema wadaɓula isamarija neɡalile esaŋena otʰile kwaɬaŋana naje ajiʃumi anoǀʰoko apʰakamisa atʰi d͡ʒesu ŋkosi kutʰe ewaɓona watʰi hambani nijoziveza kuɓapristi kwatʰi aɬaɲd͡ʒululwa eɲe jawo isiɓona ukutʰi ipʰulukisiwe jaɓuja uŋkuluŋkulu ŋezwi elikʰulu jawa ŋoɓuso ŋaseziɲaweni zakʰe imboŋa jajiŋumsamarija kepʰa ud͡ʒesu wapʰendula watʰi akuɬaɲd͡ʒululwaŋa aɓajiʃumi ɓapʰi pʰo aɓajisiʃijaɡaloluɲe aɓafuɲaniswaŋa jini aɓaɓujela uŋkuluŋkulu kupʰela wajesetʰi kuje sukuma ukukʰolwa kwakʰo eɓuzwe ŋaɓafarisi ukutʰi kaŋkuluŋkulu waɓapʰendula watʰi umbuso kaŋkuluŋkulu uɓonwa ŋameɬo futʰi kaɓajikuʃo ukutʰi ‘bekani naŋku nokuɓa ‘naŋkuja ŋokuɓa bekani kaŋkuluŋkulu upʰakatʰi wajesetʰi kuɓafundi ɓakʰe kuzakufika lapʰo nijakufisa ukuɓona luɓe luɲe zendodana jomuntu kepʰa anijikuluɓona ɓajakutʰi ‘bekani nansija bekani maniŋaji niŋalandeli ŋokuɓa ɲd͡ʒeŋoɲazi ŋǁa luɲazima kweɲe pʰansi lukʰaɲa kweɲe pʰansi joɓa ɲd͡ʒalo indodana jomuntu ŋosuku lwajo kepʰa kuǃala ukuɬupʰeka ŋokuniŋi jaliwe jilesi ɲd͡ʒeŋokuɓa emiɬeni kanowa kujakuɓa ɲd͡ʒalo nasemiɬeni jendodana jomuntu ɓaɓeɮa ɓepʰuza ɓeɡanwa ɓendiswa unowa aŋena ŋalo emkʰuɲd͡ʒini uzamǀolo waɓabubisa ɓoŋke kaɲd͡ʒalo ɲd͡ʒeŋokuɓa nasemiɬeni kaloti ɓaɓeɮa ɓepʰuza ɓetʰeŋa ɓetʰeŋisa ɓet͡ʃala ɓakʰa kepʰa ŋosuku uloti apʰuma ŋalo esodoma nesiɓaɓule kwaɓabubisa ɓoŋke kujakuɓa ɲd͡ʒalo ŋosuku ejakwambulwa ŋalo indodana jomuntu ŋalolo ojakuɓa pʰezu kwenɮu impaɬa jakʰe isenɮini kaŋeɬi ukujitʰatʰa ɲd͡ʒalo kaŋaɓujeli kʰumbulani umkaloti ofuna ukupʰila kwakʰe ujakulaɬekelwa jikʰo kepʰa olaɬekelwa jikʰo ujakukulondoloza ŋitʰi ŋaloɓo ɓusuku kujakuɓa kʰona aɓaɓili muɲe omuɲe ujakutʰatʰwa omuɲe aʃijwe kujakuɓa kʰona aɓaɓili ɓesila ndawoɲe omuɲe ujakutʰatʰwa omuɲe aʃijwe kujakuɓa kʰona aɓaɓili omuɲe ujakutʰatʰwa omuɲe aʃijwe ɓase ɓepʰendula ɓetʰi kuje kupʰi ŋkosi watʰi kuɓo lapʰo kukʰona kulapʰo amaŋǃe ejakuɓutʰana kʰona waɓalandisa wokutʰi ɓamelwe ukukʰuleka ɲd͡ʒalo ɓaŋadaŋali watʰi kwakukʰona otʰile umaɬuleli otʰile owajeŋamesaɓi uŋkuluŋkulu eŋanaki kulowo kwakukʰona futʰi owajelokʰu kuje etʰi ‘ŋizwele esitʰeni kwaɓa jisikʰatʰi eŋavumi kepʰa ŋasemuva watʰi pʰakatʰi kwakʰe ‘nakuɓa ŋiŋamesaɓi uŋkuluŋkulu ŋiŋanaki nokʰoke ŋokuɓa eŋikʰatʰaza ɲd͡ʒalo ŋijakumzwela aŋizuke ŋokufika ɲd͡ʒaloɲd͡ʒalo jajisitʰi iŋkosi jizwani okuʃiwo ŋumaɬuleli oŋaluŋile uŋkuluŋkulu kajikuɓezwela jini aɓakʰetʰiwejo ɓakʰe aɓakʰala kuje noɓusuku aɓaɓekezelele ŋitʰi uzakuɓezwela masiɲane nokʰo ŋǁa indodana jomuntu ijakufumana ukukʰolwa emɬaɓeni wajesekʰuluma kwaɓatʰile aɓaɓezetʰemba ukutʰi ɓaluŋile ɓedelela aɓaɲe eɓalandisa ŋokutʰi aɓantu aɓaɓili ɓeɲukela etʰempelini ɓeja kukʰuleka omuɲe eŋumfarisi omuɲe eŋumtʰelisi umfarisi wazikʰulekela ŋokutʰi ‘ŋkuluŋkulu ŋijakuɓoŋa ŋokuɓa ŋiŋeɲd͡ʒeŋaɓaɲe aɓantu iziɡǀ̤weleɡǀ̤wele aɓaŋaluŋile izipʰiŋi naɲd͡ʒeŋalo mtʰelisi ŋizila ukuɮa kaɓili ŋeviki ŋinikela okweʃumi kukʰo koŋke eŋinakʰo kepʰa umtʰelisi wajeŋafuni nakupʰakamisela ameɬo akʰe ŋasezulwini waʃaja isifuɓa sakʰe etʰi ‘ŋkuluŋkulu ŋihawukele ŋitʰi lo weɬela enɮini jakʰe eluŋisisiwe kunomuɲe ŋokuɓa jilowo ozipʰakamisajo uzakutʰot͡ʃiswa ozitʰoɓajo uzakupʰakaɲiswa ɓaletʰa kuje naɓantwaɲana ukuɓa aɓapʰatʰe kepʰa aɓafundi ɓekuɓona ɓaɓakʰuza kodwa ud͡ʒesu waɓaɓizela kuje watʰi vumelani aɓantwana ɓeze niŋaɓeŋǃaɓeli ŋokuɓa kaŋkuluŋkulu uŋowaɓaɲd͡ʒalo ŋiǃinisile ŋitʰi jilowo oŋamukeli kaŋkuluŋkulu ɲd͡ʒeŋomntwana aŋena umbusi otʰile wajesembuza etʰi mfundisi omuɬe ŋijakwenzani ukuɓa ŋiɮe lokupʰila okupʰakade kepʰa ud͡ʒesu watʰi kuje uŋiɓizelani ŋokutʰi ŋimuɬe kakʰo omuɬe muɲe kupʰela uŋkuluŋkulu ujajazi imijalelo ukutʰi ‘uŋapʰiŋi uŋaɓulali uŋeɓi uŋafakazi amaŋa jazisa ujiɬo noɲoko kepʰa watʰi koŋke lokʰo ŋikuɡǀ̤inile kwaseɓuʃeni ɓami ud͡ʒesu lokʰo watʰi kuje usasilalelwe iɲe tʰeŋisa ŋakʰo koŋke onakʰo waɓele aɓampofu kʰona uzakuɓa neɡuɡu uŋilandele kutʰe lokʰo wadaɓuka ŋokuɓa wajenotʰile kakʰulu ud͡ʒesu watʰi kulukʰuni kaŋakanani kwaɓa nomnotʰo ukuŋena kaŋkuluŋkulu kulula ukuɓa liŋene ŋentuɲd͡ʒa josuŋulo kunokuɓa onotʰilejo aŋene kaŋkuluŋkulu aɓezwajo ɓase ɓetʰi pʰo kuŋasindiswa ɓani kepʰa watʰi okuŋenzeki kuɓantu kuŋenzeka kuŋkuluŋkulu wajesetʰi upetru beka tʰina siʃije okwetʰu watʰi kuɓo ŋiǃinisile ŋitʰi akukʰo oʃije inɮu umkakʰe aɓafowaɓo aɓazali aɓantwana ŋeŋǁa jombuso kaŋkuluŋkulu oŋajikwamukeliswa okupʰindwe kaniŋi sikʰatʰi naseŋkatʰini ezajo ukupʰila okupʰakade wajeseɓasondeza kuje aɓajiʃumi watʰi kuɓo bekani sikʰupʰukela ed͡ʒerusalema koŋke okulot͡ʃwe ŋaɓaprofetʰi ŋendodana jomuntu kujakuɡǀ̤waliseka ŋokuɓa izakukʰaʃelwa kwaɓezizwe ikxolodelwe iduɲazwe ikʰafulelwe ŋamatʰe ɓajiʃaje ɓajiɓulale kepʰa ŋosuku lwesitʰatʰu kepʰa ɓona kaɓaǃondaŋa lutʰo lwalokʰo lalifiɬakele kuɓo aɓakuǃondaŋa oɓekuʃiwo kwatʰi ed͡ʒeriko impumputʰe etʰile jajiɬezi ŋasenɮeleni iŋǁiɓa isizwa isiǁuku siɮula jaɓuza ukutʰi kujini lokʰu ɓase ɓejit͡ʃela ukutʰi kuɮula ud͡ʒesu wasenazaretʰa jajisimemeza itʰi d͡ʒesu ndodana kadavide ŋihawukele aɓaɓehamba pʰambili ɓajikʰuza ukuɓa itʰule kepʰa kwajikʰona kakʰulu jona itʰi ndodana kadavide ŋihawukele wemake ud͡ʒesu wajala ukuɓa iletʰwe kuje isisondele wajiɓuza watʰi ufuna ukuɓa ŋikwenzeleni jatʰi ŋkosi ukuɓa ŋiɓone ud͡ʒesu watʰi kujo ɓona ukukʰolwa kwakʰo jajisiɓona kʰona lapʰo jamlandela uŋkuluŋkulu naɓantu ɓoŋke ɓekuɓona ɓamnika uŋkuluŋkulu waŋena ed͡ʒeriko wadaɓula kʰona beka kwakukʰona iɡama lajo liŋuzakewu iŋumtʰelisi omkʰulu iǀeɓile jajifuna ud͡ʒesu ukutʰi uŋuɓani jaɬuleka ŋeŋǁa jesiǁuku ŋokuɓa jajimfuʃane jaɡid͡ʒimela pʰambili jakʰwela emtʰombeni ukuɓa ŋokuɓa eɓezakuɮula ŋakʰona esefikile ud͡ʒesu kulejo wabeka pʰezulu watʰi kujo zakewu ʃeʃa weɬe ŋokuɓa namuɬa ŋimelwe ukuɬala enɮini jakʰo waʃeʃa weɬa ŋokutʰokoza kutʰe ɓekuɓona ɓakʰonona ɓoŋke ɓatʰi uje kuŋenisa ejisoni kodwa uzakewu watʰi eŋkosini beka ŋkosi ŋipʰa aɓampofu iŋǁeɲe jempaɬa jami kutʰi ŋimapʰuǀile ŋamaǀeɓo ŋijiɓujisa ipʰindwe ud͡ʒesu watʰi kuje namuɬa nɮu lokʰu naje ejindodana kaaɓrahama ŋokuɓa indodana jomuntu okulaɬekilejo kutʰe ukuɓa ɓakuzwe lokʰo ŋokuɓa eɓeseduze ned͡ʒerusalema naŋokuɓa ɓeɓetʰi kaŋkuluŋkulu uzakuɓonakala masiɲane watʰike umuntu otʰile woɬaŋa olukʰulu waja ejozitʰatʰela aɓuje wajeseɓiza iziŋǀeku zakʰe ezijiʃumi aɓajiʃumi watʰi ‘hweɓani ŋaɓo ŋize ŋiɓuje kepʰa aɓantu ɓomuzi wakʰe ɓaɓemzonda ɓatʰuma amaŋǁusa kwakʰe ɓetʰi ‘asitʰandi ukuɓa aɓuse pʰezu kwetʰu kwatʰi eseɓujile ekutʰatʰeni watʰi aziɓizelwe kuje ziŋǀeku aɓezinike ukuɓa ukutʰi jilejo nalejo ŋokuhweɓa javelake ejokuǃala jatʰi ‘ŋkosi wakʰo aɓajiʃumi watʰi kujo ‘kuɬeke ŋǀeku enɬe lokʰu ufuɲanwe utʰembekile kokuŋǀiɲane uzakuɓusa pʰezu ejiʃumi jafika nejesiɓili jatʰi ‘umina wakʰo ŋkosi aɓajisiɬanu watʰi nakulejo ‘nawe jiɓa pʰezu ejisiɬanu kwafika neɲe jatʰi ‘ŋkosi naŋu wakʰo eɓeŋimkʰwezile esoŋwe endwaŋwini ŋokuɓa ɓeŋikwesaɓa lokʰu uŋumuntu olukʰuni utʰaɓatʰa oŋakuɓekaŋa oŋakuɬwaɲelaŋa watʰi kujo ‘ŋizakukwaɬulela ŋomlomo wakʰo ŋǀeku uɓuwazi ukuɓa ŋiŋumumtu olukʰuni ŋitʰaɓatʰa eŋiŋakuɓekaŋa ŋivuna eŋiŋakuɬwaɲelaŋa awufakaŋa ŋani jami ebaŋe ŋaɓe ŋijiɓizile kaɲe wajesetʰi kwaɓaɓemi kʰona ‘mapʰuǀeni aɓajiʃumi kepʰa ɓatʰi kuje ‘ŋkosi aɓajiʃumi ŋitʰi jilowo onakʰo ujakupʰiwa kepʰa oŋenakʰo ujakwapʰuǀwa nalokʰo anakʰo kodwa zitʰa ezaziŋatʰandi ukuɓa ŋiɓuse pʰezu ziletʰeni lapʰa niziɓulale pʰambi eseʃilo lokʰo waǃʰuɓekela pʰambili wakʰupʰukela ed͡ʒerusalema kwatʰi eɓetfaɡe naseɓetʰanija ŋasentaɓeni etʰiwa ejemiŋǃumo watʰuma aɓaɓili kuɓafundi ɓakʰe etʰi hambani nije obekene notʰi ukuɓa niŋene itʰole lemboŋolo likʰulekiwe okuŋazaŋe kuɬale litʰukululeni nililetʰe uma eniɓuza etʰi ‘nilitʰukululelani anotʰi ‘iŋkosi ijalidiŋa aɓaɓetʰuɲiwe ɓahambake ɓafumana kuɲd͡ʒeŋokuʃo kwakʰe kuɓo kutʰe ɓesalitʰukulula itʰole aɓaninilo ɓatʰi kuɓo nilitʰukululelani itʰole ɓatʰi iŋkosi ijalidiŋa ɓase ɓeliletʰa kud͡ʒesu ɓaɓeka iziŋuɓo zaɓo pʰezu kwetʰole ɓamkʰwelisa ud͡ʒesu esahamba ɓaɓenɮala iziŋuɓo zaɓo enɮeleni esesondela ekweɬeleni kwentaɓa jemiŋǃumo isiǁuku soŋke saɓafundi saǃala ukutʰokoza uŋkuluŋkulu ŋezwi elikʰulu ŋemiseɓenzi joŋke jamanɮa esijiɓonilejo sitʰi uɓusisiwe umbusi ozajo eɡameni leŋkosi ukutʰula neŋkazimulo kwelipʰezulu aɓaɲe ɓaɓafarisi ɓesesiǁukwini ɓatʰi kuje mfundisi ɓakʰuze aɓafundi ɓakʰo wapʰendula watʰi ŋitʰi uma ɓetʰula laɓa amat͡ʃe kwatʰi ewuɓona wawukʰalela watʰi seŋatʰi ŋa ŋalolu okokutʰula kepʰa kalokʰu kufiɬakele emeɬweni akʰo ŋokuɓa ujakufikelwa jizinsuku lapʰo izitʰa zijakukukaka ŋodoŋa zikuhaǃe ŋǁazoŋke pʰansi naɓantwana aɓakuwe ziŋaʃiji it͡ʃe pʰezu kwet͡ʃe pʰakatʰi kwakʰo ŋokuɓa uŋasazaŋa isikʰatʰi sokuhaɲd͡ʒelwa kwakʰo waŋena etʰempelini waǃala ukuǁoʃa aɓatʰeŋisajo watʰi kuɓo kulot͡ʃiwe ukutʰi ‘inɮu jami ijakuɓa jinɮu jokukʰuleka kepʰa nijenze waɓapʰaŋi wajefundisa etʰempelini imiɬa ŋemiɬa kepʰa aɓapristi aɓakʰulu naɓabali nezikʰulu zaɓantu ɓafuna kodwa ɓaɓeŋatʰoli ukutʰi ɓaŋenzani ŋokuɓa aɓantu ɓoŋke ɓaɓeɓambelela kuje ɓemuzwa kwatʰi ŋoluɲe aɓantu etʰempelini eʃumajela ivaŋeli aɓapristi aɓakʰulu naɓabali ɓekaɲe namaluŋa ɓamvukela ɓakʰuluma ɓatʰi kuje sit͡ʃele ukutʰi lokʰu ŋaɡuɲa nokuɓa ŋuɓani ɡuɲa wapʰendula watʰi kuɓo nami ŋizakuniɓuza niŋit͡ʃele ukubapatʰiza kukad͡ʒohane kuɓantu ɓazinɮisana ɓodwa ɓatʰi uma sitʰi ‘ezulwini uzakutʰi ‘anikʰolwaŋa ŋuje ŋani kepʰa sitʰi ‘kuɓantu aɓantu ɓoŋke ɓazakusikʰanda ŋamat͡ʃe ŋokuɓa ɓakʰoliwe ukutʰi ud͡ʒohane uŋumprofetʰi ɓase ɓepʰendula ukutʰi aɓazi lapʰo kʰona ud͡ʒesu wajesetʰi kuɓo namike aŋinit͡ʃeli ukutʰi ŋenza lokʰu ŋaɡuɲa wajeseǃala etʰi kuɓantu umuntu wat͡ʃala wasiǃaʃisa kuɓalimi waja kweliɲe isikʰatʰi ŋeŋkatʰi efanelejo wajesetʰumela iŋǀeku kuɓalimi ukuɓa ɓamnike ezitʰelweni kepʰa aɓalimi ɓajiʃaja ɓajimukisa wapʰinda watʰuma eɲe iŋǀeku nalejo ɓajiʃaja ɓajidumaza ɓajimukisa wajesepʰinda etʰuma nejesitʰatʰu ɓajilimaza ɓajipʰonsa ŋapʰanɮe kʰona watʰi ‘ŋizakwenze ɲd͡ʒani ŋizakutʰuma jami etʰandekajo mɬawumbe ɓazakujazisa kepʰa aɓalimi ɓejiɓona ɓakʰulumisana ɓatʰi ‘lo ujinɮalifa masijiɓulale ukuɓa liɓe ŋeletʰu ɓajipʰonsa ŋapʰanɮe ɓajiɓulala ŋakʰoke ɲd͡ʒani kuɓo uzakuza aɓabubise laɓo ɓalimi aɓaɲe ɓekuzwa ɓatʰi ǃʰa makuŋaɓi ɲd͡ʒalo kepʰa waɓabeka watʰi jini pʰo lokʰu okulot͡ʃiwejo ukutʰi ‘it͡ʃe aɓaliŋǃaɓajo aɓakʰi laɓa jinɬoko jeɡumbi jilowo owajo pʰezu t͡ʃe ujakupʰoɬozwa kepʰa elijakuwela pʰezu kwakʰe lijakumǀolisa aɓabali naɓapristi ɓafuna kʰona lapʰo kepʰa ɓesaɓa aɓantu ŋokuɓa ɓazi ukutʰi uwukʰulumile ŋaɓo ɓamǃapʰela ɓatʰuma izinɬoli eziziʃaja aɓaluŋilejo ukuɓa ɓamhile ŋezwi lakʰe ɓaze ɓamkʰapʰele emanɮeni naseɡuɲeni ɓambuzake ɓatʰi mfundisi sijazi ukutʰi ukʰuluma ŋokuǃondilejo awukʰetʰi ɓuso ɓamuntu kepʰa inɮela kaŋkuluŋkulu ŋokuǃinisilejo sivuɲelwe ukutʰela kukesari ǃʰa kepʰa eǃonda uɓuǃili ɓaɓo watʰi kuɓo ŋiɓoniseni udenariju kaɓani ɓatʰi okakesari wajesetʰi kuɓo ŋakʰoke ukesari okukakesari noŋkuluŋkulu okukaŋkuluŋkulu aɓaze ɓaɓa namanɮa ŋezwi lakʰe pʰambi kwaɓantu ɓamaŋala ŋokupʰendula kwakʰe ɓatʰula kwase kuje aɓatʰile ɓaɓasadusi aɓatʰi akukʰo kwaɓafilejo ɓambuza ɓatʰi mfundisi umose wasiloɓela ukutʰi umfowaɓo kepʰa eŋenamntwana umfowaɓo makamtʰatʰe umkakʰe umfowaɓo kwakukʰona ezijisikʰombisa owokuǃala watʰatʰa eŋenamntwana nowesiɓili nowesitʰatʰu wamtʰatʰa kaɲd͡ʒaloke aɓajisikʰombisa ɓafa ɓeŋaʃijaŋa ɓantwana ukuɡǀ̤ina ŋakʰoke ujakuɓa ŋumfazi wamupʰi kuɓo lokʰu aɓajisikʰombisa ɓaɓe naje eŋumkaɓo ud͡ʒesu watʰi kuɓo aɓantwana ɓale ŋkatʰi ɓajaɡanwa ɓajendiswa kepʰa laɓo aɓazakutʰiwa ɓafanele ukufiɲelela kulejo ŋkatʰi kwaɓafilejo kaɓaɡanwa kaɓendiswa ŋokuɓa ɓaŋeɓuje ɓafe ɓaɲd͡ʒeŋeziŋelosi ɓaŋaɓantwana ɓakaŋkuluŋkulu ɓeŋaɓantwana ɓokuvuka kepʰa ukutʰi ɓajavuswa aɓafilejo nomose wakuɓonakalisa esiɬaɬeni lapʰo ejiɓiza iŋkosi ŋokutʰi uŋkuluŋkulu kaaɓrahama noŋkuluŋkulu kaisaka noŋkuluŋkulu kad͡ʒakoɓe uŋkuluŋkulu kasije owaɓafilejo owaɓapʰilajo ŋokuɓa ɓoŋke ɓapʰila kuje aɓatʰile ɓaɓabali ɓapʰendula ɓatʰi mfundisi ukʰulume kaɬe ŋokuɓa ɓaɓeŋasenasiɓindi lutʰo wajesetʰi kuɓo ɓaʃo kaɲd͡ʒani ukutʰi ukristu ujindodana kadavide lokʰu udavide uǃoɓo utʰi eŋǀwadini jamahuɓo ‘iŋkosi jatʰi eŋkosini jami ɬala ŋakwesokunene ŋize ŋiɓeke izitʰa zakʰo ziɓe jisenaɓelo seziɲawo zakʰo ŋakʰo udavide ŋokutʰi iŋkosi pʰo ujindodana jakʰe kaɲd͡ʒani ɓesalalele aɓantu ɓoŋke watʰi kuɓafundi ɓakʰe ǁwajani aɓabali aɓafuna ɓembetʰe iziŋuɓo ɓetʰanda ukuɓiŋelelwa eziɡǀ̤awini nokuɬala pʰambili emasinaɡoɡeni eziŋenɬa ekuɮeni aɓaɮa izinɮu zaɓafelokazi ɓekʰuleka isikʰatʰi ŋokuzenzisa laɓa ɓajakwamukeliswa ukulaɬwa okukʰulu kwatʰi ebeka waɓona aɓaǀeɓilejo ɓeɓeka jaɓo empʰoŋolweni waɓona otʰile eɓeka kʰona amafadiŋi amaɓili watʰi ŋiǃinisile ŋitʰi lo uɓeke okuniŋi kunaɓo ɓoŋke ŋokuɓa ɓoŋke laɓa ɓaɓeka kokuǀʰiǀʰimilejo kwaɓo kepʰa jena eɓumpofini ɓakʰe uɓeke koŋke aɓepʰila ŋakʰo ɓesakʰuluma aɓaɲe ŋetʰempeli ukutʰi liɬot͡ʃiswe ŋamat͡ʃe amaɬe naŋezipʰo watʰi kuɓo kujakufika lapʰo kuŋajikuʃijwa kulokʰu enikuɓonajo it͡ʃe pʰezu kwet͡ʃe eliŋajikudilizelwa pʰansi ɓase ɓembuza ɓetʰi mfundisi lokʰu kujakuɓa nesiɓonakaliso sijakuɓa jini lapʰo sekujakwenzeka lokʰu watʰi ǃapʰelani niŋadukiswa ŋokuɓa kujakuza aɓaniŋi ŋeɡama ɓatʰi ‘ŋiŋuje ɓatʰi futʰi ‘isikʰatʰi maniŋaɓalandeli ŋǁa ŋezimpi nezijalujalu niŋetʰuki ŋokuɓa ukuɓa lokʰo kuǃala kepʰa ukupʰela akukaɓikʰo masiɲane kʰona watʰi kuɓo isizwe sijakuvukela kujakuɓa kʰona okukʰulu komɬaɓa nobiǀi nenɮala ŋezindawo kuɓe kʰona ezesaɓekajo neziɓonakaliso eziŋkulu kepʰa ŋapʰambi kwakʰo koŋke lokʰo ɓajakuniɓamba ɓaniziŋele ɓanikʰapʰele emasinaɡoɡeni nasematiloŋweni ɓanijise pʰambi kwamakʰosi naɓaɓusi ŋeŋǁa jeɡama kujakuneɬela kuɓe ŋuɓufakazi ŋakʰo kuɡǀ̤ineni ezinɬizijweni ukuɓa niŋazinɮi ŋapʰambili enijakuzipʰendulela ŋakʰo ŋokuɓa ŋijakuninika nokuɬakanipʰa aɓaŋemelane nakʰo ɓakupʰike ɓoŋke aɓajimpi jeɓo nijakukʰaʃelwa naŋaɓazali naɓafowenu neziɬoɓo naɓaŋane aɓaɲe ɓenu ɓajakuɓulawa jiɓo nijakuzondwa jiɓo ɓoŋke ŋeŋǁa jeɡama akujikulaɬeka lwekʰanda ŋokukʰutʰazela nijakuzuza imipʰefumulo jenu kepʰa ŋǁa niɓona id͡ʒerusalema lihaǃiwe jizimpi jazini ukutʰi ukuǀʰitʰwa kʰona aɓased͡ʒudija maɓaɓalekele ezintaɓeni aɓapʰakatʰi ɓapʰume aɓasemapʰanɮeni ɓaŋaŋeni ŋokuɓa zijizinsuku ukuɓa kuɡǀ̤waliseke koŋke okulot͡ʃiwejo maje kwaɓakʰulelwejo naɓaŋǀelisajo ŋalezo ŋokuɓa kujakuɓa kʰona ukuɬupʰeka okukʰulu emɬaɓeni nentukutʰelo pʰezu ɓajakuwa ɓeɮiwa jiŋkemba ɓatʰuɲd͡ʒelwe zoŋke id͡ʒerusalema lijakuɲatʰelwa pʰansi ŋaɓezizwe kuɡǀ̤waliseke izikʰatʰi zaɓezizwe kujakuɓa kʰona iziɓonakaliso elaŋeni naseɲaŋeni naseziŋkaɲezini nasemɬaɓeni lujakweɬela ziǁakeke ŋokuduma kolwanɮe aɓantu ɓapʰele amanɮa ŋokwesaɓa naŋokubeka umɬaɓa ŋokuɓa amanɮa ajakuɲakaziswa kʰona ɓajakujiɓona indodana jomuntu inamanɮa neŋkazimulo eŋkulu kepʰa ŋǁa kuǃala lokʰo nipʰakamise amakʰanda ŋokuɓa ukukʰululwa waɓalandisa wokutʰi bekani umkʰiwane nemitʰi joŋke ŋǁa isiɬuma nijaɓona ŋokwenu ukutʰi iɬoɓo kaɲd͡ʒalo ŋǁa niɓona jazini ukutʰi kaŋkuluŋkulu ŋiǃinisile ŋitʰi lesi asijikuɮula kuŋakenzeki koŋke kujakuɮula nomɬaɓa kepʰa aɮula ǁwajani ukuɓa izinɬizijo ziŋasindwa ŋukuminza okwalokʰu kupʰila niŋazelele ŋokuɓa lujakufika ɲd͡ʒeŋoɡiɓe pʰezu kwaɓo ɓoŋke aɓaɬezi emɬaɓeni woŋke ŋakʰo ŋesikʰatʰi soŋke nikʰuleke ukuɓa niɓe namanɮa okupʰepʰa kukʰo koŋke lokʰu okujakwenzeka pʰambi kwendodana jomuntu ɲd͡ʒalo wajefundisa etʰempelini kepʰa kusiɬwa wajepʰuma ajokulala entaɓeni etʰiwa ejemiŋǃumo ekuseni aɓantu ɓoŋke ɓeza kuje etʰempelini kwasondela umkʰosi wesiŋkwa esiŋenamvuɓelo otʰiwa ipʰasika aɓapristi aɓakʰulu naɓabali ɓafuna ukuɓa ɓaŋambulala kaɲd͡ʒani ŋokuɓa ɓaɓesaɓa aɓantu kepʰa usatʰane waŋena kud͡ʒuda otʰiwa uiskarijotʰe eŋowaɓajiʃumi wasuka wakʰuluma naɓapristi aɓakʰulu ŋokutʰi aŋamkʰapʰela kaɲd͡ʒani kuɓo ɓatʰokoza ɓavumelana naje wavumake itʰuɓa lokumkʰapʰela kuɓo siŋekʰo isiǁuku lwase lwesiŋkwa esiŋenamvuɓelo ukuɓa kuɬat͡ʃwe ŋalo ipʰasika watʰuma opetru nod͡ʒohane watʰi hambani nije ukusiluŋisela ipʰasika ukuɓa siɮe ɓatʰi kuje utʰanda ukuɓa sikuluŋiselepʰi watʰi kuɓo bekani seniŋene nijakuɬaŋana otʰwele jamanzi nije enɮini aŋena kujo nitʰi kumnininɮu ‘utʰi umfundisi lipʰi lokuŋenisa lapʰo ŋiŋaɮela kʰona ipʰasika naɓafundi ɓami lowoke uzakunikʰombisa elikʰulu elipʰezulu elenɮelwejo luŋiselani lapʰo ɓasuka ɓafumana kuɲd͡ʒeŋokuʃo kwakʰe kuɓo ɓase ɓeluŋisa ipʰasika kwatʰi ukuɓa isikʰatʰi waɬala pʰansi naɓapʰostoli kaɲe naje wajesetʰi kuɓo ŋiŋǁanele nokuŋǁanela ukuɮa pʰasika ŋiŋakaɬupʰeki ŋokuɓa ŋitʰi aŋisajikuliɮa ŋempela liɡǀ̤waliseke kaŋkuluŋkulu wamukela isit͡ʃa waɓoŋa watʰi tʰaɓatʰani lokʰu naɓelane ŋokuɓa ŋitʰi maɲd͡ʒe aŋisajikupʰuza okwesitʰelo kaŋkuluŋkulu wajesetʰaɓatʰa isiŋkwa waɓoŋa wasiɬepʰula waɓanika watʰi lokʰu kuŋumzimba jenzani lokʰu ukuɓa niŋikʰumbule kaɲd͡ʒaloke nesit͡ʃa kokuɮa etʰi lesi sit͡ʃa sijisivumelwano esiʃa eɡazini elitʰululelwa kepʰa bekani isanɮa soŋikʰapʰelajo ŋokuɓa indodana jomuntu ɲd͡ʒeŋokumisiwejo kepʰa maje ekʰaʃelwa ŋaje ɓase ɓeǃala ukuɓuzana ɓodwa ukutʰi kuŋase kuɓe ŋuɓani kuɓo lokʰo kwavela nokupʰikisana pʰakatʰi kwaɓo kokutʰi ŋumupʰi kuɓo oŋatʰiwa omkʰulu wajesetʰi kuɓo aɓaɓusi ɓezizwe ɓazenza amakʰosi pʰezu nezipʰatʰimanɮa zitʰiwa aɓazenzela okuɬe kepʰa aniɲd͡ʒalo omkʰulu makaɓe ɲd͡ʒeŋomŋǀiɲane noɓusajo makaɓe ɲd͡ʒeŋokʰonzajo ŋokuɓa ŋumupʰi omkʰulu oɬezi ekuɮeni okʰonzajo akusije oɬezi ekuɮeni kepʰa ŋipʰakatʰi ɲd͡ʒeŋokʰonzajo ninake niŋaɓaɓekʰutʰazela ekuliŋweni naɲd͡ʒeŋokuɓa uɓaɓa eŋimisele ŋinimisela ukuɓa niɮe nipʰuze nijakuɬala eziɬalweni zoɓukʰosi naɬulele ezijiʃumi zakwaisrajeli simoni simoni beka usatʰane ukuɓa aniɬuŋe ɲd͡ʒeŋokolweni kepʰa ŋikuŋǁusele ukuɓa ukukʰolwa kwakʰo kuŋapʰeli ŋǁa usupʰendukile uǃinise aɓafowenu watʰi kuje ŋkosi ŋiluŋele ukuja nasetiloŋweni wajesetʰi ŋijakut͡ʃela petru ukutʰi iǃʰude alijikukʰala namɬaɲd͡ʒe uŋakaŋipʰiki katʰatʰu ukutʰi awuŋazi watʰi kuɓo mɬa ŋinitʰuma niŋenasikʰwama najika naziǀatʰulo utʰo ɓatʰi lutʰo wajesetʰi kuɓo kepʰa maɲd͡ʒe onesikʰwama kasitʰatʰe nejika futʰi oswelajo katʰeŋise ŋeŋuɓo jakʰe atʰeŋe iŋkemba ŋokuɓa ŋitʰi kumelwe ukuɡǀ̤waliseka lokʰo okulot͡ʃiwejo kokutʰi ‘waɓalwa kaɲe ŋokuɓa okuǃondene sekujapʰelela ɓase ɓetʰi ŋkosi beka iziŋkemba watʰi kuɓo kwanele wajesepʰuma waja entaɓeni jemiŋǃumo ɲd͡ʒeŋomkʰuɓa wakʰe naɓafundi ɓakʰe ɓamlandela esefikile watʰi kuɓo kʰulekani ukuɓa niŋaŋeni ekuliŋweni wamoɲuka kuɓo kuŋatʰi iɓaŋa lokupʰonsa it͡ʃe waɡuǃa pʰansi wakʰuleka watʰi ɓaɓa utʰanda sit͡ʃa nokʰo makuŋenziwa jami ejakʰo kwaɓonakala kuje iŋelosi imǃinisa esosizini wakʰuleka eǃinisela izitʰukutʰuku zakʰe zaɓa ɲd͡ʒeŋamatʰonsi eɡazi aǀonsela emɬaɓatʰini esesukume ekukʰulekeni kuɓafundi ɓakʰe waɓafumana ɓelele ŋokudaɓuka watʰi kuɓo nilaleleni vukani nikʰuleke ukuɓa niŋaŋeni ekuliŋweni esakʰuluma beka isiǁuku naje otʰiwa ud͡ʒuda omuɲe waɓajiʃumi wajehamba pʰambi kwaɓo kud͡ʒesu ukumaŋa kepʰa ud͡ʒesu watʰi kuje d͡ʒuda ujajikʰapʰela indodana jomuntu ŋokujaŋa kutʰe aɓaɓeŋakuje seɓeɓona ɓatʰi ŋkosi siɡaɮe ŋeŋkemba omuɲe otʰile kuɓo wajiɡaɮa iŋǀeku jompristi omkʰulu wajiŋǃuma inɮeɓe jokunene kepʰa ud͡ʒesu watʰatʰa watʰi musani wajipʰatʰa inɮeɓe wajipʰolisa watʰi ud͡ʒesu kuɓapristi aɓakʰulu zetʰempeli namaluŋa aɓaɓeze kuje nipʰumile kuŋatʰi kumpʰaŋi nipʰetʰe iziŋkemba ɓeŋinani imiɬa ŋemiɬa etʰempelini anelulaŋa zanɮa kepʰa lokʰu kujihora namanɮa oɓumɲama ɓase ɓembamba ɓamuka naje ɓamusa enɮini jompristi omkʰulu upetru seɓeɓasile pʰakatʰi eɡǀ̤ekeni ɓaɬala pʰansi ndawoɲe upetru waɬala pʰakatʰi kwaɓo intombazana etʰile eɬezi ŋasemlilweni jamɡǃ̤olozela jatʰi nalona uɓe naje kepʰa wapʰika watʰi sifazane aŋimazi emva kwesikʰaʃana omuɲe watʰi nawe uŋomuɲe waɓo kepʰa upetru watʰi muntundini aŋisije sekuɮulile okuŋatʰi liɲe omuɲe waǃinisa watʰi impela uɓe naje ŋokuɓa futʰi uŋowaseɡalile kepʰa upetru watʰi muntundini aŋikwazi ukutʰi utʰini masiɲane esakʰuluma lakʰala iǃʰude iŋkosi jajisipʰenduka jambheka upetru upetru walikʰumbula leŋkosi ɲd͡ʒeŋokuɓa itʰe kuje iǃʰude liŋakakʰali namɬaɲd͡ʒe uzakuŋipʰika katʰatʰu wapʰumela pʰanɮe wakʰala kamuɲu amadoda aɓembambile ud͡ʒesu ambhiŋǃa emʃaja ammboza uɓuso etʰi profetʰa ukutʰi ŋuɓani okuʃajilejo nokuɲe okuniŋi akukʰuluma kuje emtʰuka kwatʰi kwaɓutʰana amaluŋa aɓantu naɓapristi aɓakʰulu naɓabali usimoni petru eneŋkemba wajihoʃa wajiɡeŋǀa iŋǀeku jompristi omkʰulu wajiŋǃuma inɮeɓe jokunene iɡama leŋǀeku laliŋumalkusi kʰona ud͡ʒesu watʰi kupetru faka iŋkemba emɡoɮeni wajo aŋijikusipʰuza isit͡ʃa aŋinike uɓaɓa ɲd͡ʒaloke isiɡaɓa jeŋkuluŋwane nezikʰonzi zaɓad͡ʒuda ɓambamba ud͡ʒesu ɓambopʰa ɓaǃala ɓamjisa kuanase ŋokuɓa eŋumukʰwe kakajafase oɓeŋumpristi omkʰulu mɲaka ukajafase ŋuje aɓad͡ʒuda ŋokutʰi kuɓaluŋele ukuɓa aɓe muɲe ŋeŋǁa jesizwe usimoni petru ud͡ʒesu nomuɲe lowo wajaziwa ŋumpristi omkʰulu waŋena nod͡ʒesu eɡǀ̤ekeni omkʰulu kepʰa upetru wajemi ŋapʰanɮe emɲaŋo wapʰumake omuɲe ŋumpristi omkʰulu wakʰuluma womɲaŋo wamŋenisa upetru intombazana emɲaŋo jajisitʰi kupetru imbala awusije owaɓafundi ɓalowo watʰi jena aŋisije kwakumi kʰona iziŋǀeku nezikʰonzi ziɓasile wamalaɬe ŋokuɓa kwakumakʰaza zotʰa nopetru wajenazo otʰa kepʰa omkʰulu waɓuza ud͡ʒesu ŋaɓafundi ɓakʰe naŋemfundiso jakʰe ud͡ʒesu wampʰendula watʰi ŋikʰulumile oɓala ŋezikʰatʰi zoŋke ɓeŋifundisa esinaɡoɡeni nasetʰempelini lapʰo aɓad͡ʒuda ɓoŋke ɓeɓutʰana kʰona aŋikʰulumaŋa lutʰo ŋasese uɓuzelani ɓuza kulaɓo aɓezwile lokʰo eŋakukʰuluma kuɓo beka ɓona ɓajakwazi eŋakuʃojo esaʃo lokʰo esiɲe isikʰonzi kʰona ud͡ʒesu satʰi upʰendula omkʰulu kaɲd͡ʒalo ud͡ʒesu wasipʰendula watʰi uma ŋikʰulume kaɓi ŋaloɓo ɓuɓi kukuɬe uŋiʃajelani uanase wamtʰumela eɓoʃiwe kukajafase omkʰulu kepʰa usimoni petru wajemi otʰa ɓatʰike kuje imbala awusije owaɓafundi ɓakʰe wapʰika jena watʰi aŋisije eɲe jeziŋǀeku omkʰulu ejisiɬoɓo onɮeɓe jaso upetru aɓejiŋǃumile jatʰi aŋikuɓonaŋa jini unaje waɓuje wapʰika upetru masiɲane lakʰala iǃʰude ɓase ɓekʰipʰa ud͡ʒesu kukajafase ɓemjisa enɮini jokwaɬulela kepʰa ɓona kaɓaŋenaŋa eŋǃaɓeni ukuɓa ɓaŋaŋǀ̤oli ɓaɓe nokuɮa ipʰasika kʰona upilatu wapʰumela kuɓo watʰi nimtʰwesa ǀala ɓapʰendula ɓatʰi kuje uma eɓeŋesije okuɓi ŋa siŋamletʰaŋa kʰona upilatu watʰi kuɓo mtʰatʰeni nimaɬulele ŋomtʰetʰo ɓatʰi kuje aɓad͡ʒuda asivuɲelwe ukuɓulala ukuɓa kuɡǀ̤waliseke likad͡ʒesu aliʃilo lapʰa eɓonisa ukutʰi ujakufa ŋokufa okuɲd͡ʒani upilatu waɓuje waŋena eŋǃaɓeni waɓiza ud͡ʒesu watʰi kuje wena ujiŋkosi jaɓad͡ʒuda ud͡ʒesu wapʰendula watʰi uziʃolo lokʰu kuʃo aɓaɲe ŋami upilatu wapʰendula watʰi kanti ŋiŋumd͡ʒuda jini isizwe naɓapristi aɓakʰulu ɓakunikezele ud͡ʒesu wapʰendula watʰi umbuso uma uɓuŋowaleli izikʰonzi zazijakulwa ukuɓa ŋiŋanikezelwa kuɓad͡ʒuda kepʰa kalokʰu owalapʰa wajesetʰi upilatu kuje kanti nokʰo ujiŋkosi ud͡ʒesu wapʰendula watʰi uʃo kʰona ŋijiŋkosi ŋizalelwe lokʰo ŋafikela lokʰo ukuɓa ŋifakazele iǃiniso ɓoŋke aɓeǃiniso ɓajalizwa watʰi upilatu kuje iǃiniso lijini eseʃilo lokʰo waɓuje wapʰumela kuɓad͡ʒuda watʰi kuɓo aŋifumani ǀala kuje kepʰa lokuɓa ŋinikʰululele omuɲe ŋepʰasika ŋakʰo nijatʰanda ukuɓa ŋinikʰululele iŋkosi jaɓad͡ʒuda kʰona ɓaɓuje ɓamemeza ɓoŋke ɓatʰi ǃʰa uɓaraɓa kepʰa uɓaraɓa wajeŋumpʰaŋi upilatu wajesemtʰatʰa ud͡ʒesu wamʃaja amaɓutʰo umǃʰele ekʰanda lakʰe amembatʰisa iŋuɓo eɓuɓende aja kuje atʰi ɓajede ŋkosi jaɓad͡ʒuda ammukula upilatu waɓuje wapʰuma watʰi kuɓo bekani ŋimkʰipʰela ukuɓa aŋifumani ǀala kuje wajesepʰuma ud͡ʒesu etʰwele umǃʰele neŋuɓo eɓuɓende watʰi kuɓo upilatu bekani ɓatʰi ɓembona aɓapristi aɓakʰulu nezikʰonzi ɓamemeza ɓatʰi mbetʰele mbetʰele esipʰambanweni upilatu watʰi kuɓo mtʰatʰeni nimbetʰele esipʰambanweni ŋokuɓa aŋifumani ǀala kuje kepʰa aɓad͡ʒuda ɓampʰendula ɓatʰi sinomtʰetʰo tʰina ŋalo mtʰetʰo ŋokuɓa indodana kaŋkuluŋkulu kutʰe upilatu kwajikʰona esaɓa kakʰulu waɓuje waŋena eŋǃaɓeni watʰi kud͡ʒesu uŋowapʰi kepʰa ud͡ʒesu kampʰendulaŋa kʰona watʰi upilatu kuje awukʰulumi awazi ukutʰi ŋinamanɮa okukukʰulula ŋinamanɮa futʰi okukuɓetʰela esipʰambanweni ud͡ʒesu wapʰendula watʰi ŋaɓe awunamanɮa pʰezu ukuɓa awuwanikwaŋa ŋapʰezulu ŋalokʰoke oŋinikele esikʰulu ŋalokʰo upilatu wajefuna ukumkʰulula kepʰa aɓad͡ʒuda ɓamemeza ɓatʰi uma ukʰulula awusije umɬoɓo kakesari iŋkosi nokesari kutʰe upilatu wamkʰipʰela ŋapʰanɮe ud͡ʒesu waɬala esiɬalweni sokwaɬulela etʰiwa eɡandajwe ŋamat͡ʃe ŋesiheɓeru iɡaɓatʰa kwakuŋolokuluŋisela ipʰasika kuŋatʰi lesitʰupʰa watʰi kuɓad͡ʒuda bekani iŋkosi jenu ŋakʰo ɓamemeza ɓatʰi susa mbetʰele esipʰambanweni watʰi kuɓo upilatu ŋiɓetʰele iŋkosi jenu aɓapristi aɓakʰulu ɓapʰendula ɓatʰi asinaŋkosi ukesari kupʰela wajesemnikela kuɓo ukuɓa aɓetʰelwe esipʰambanweni ɓamtʰatʰake ud͡ʒesu ɓahamba naje wapʰuma ezitʰwalele isipʰambano waja etʰiwa indawo jekʰanda etʰiwa ŋesiheɓeru iɡolɡotʰa ɓambetʰela kʰona naɓaɲe aɓaɓili kaɲe naje ŋalapʰa naŋalapʰa ud͡ʒesu epʰakatʰi kepʰa upilatu waloɓa wasiɓeka esipʰambanweni kwakulot͡ʃiwe ukutʰi ud͡ʒesu wasenazaretʰa iŋkosi jaɓad͡ʒuda kʰona aɓaniŋi ɓaɓad͡ʒuda ɓafunda ŋokuɓa lejo lapʰo ud͡ʒesu waɓetʰelwa kʰona esipʰambanweni jajiseduze kwakulot͡ʃiwe ŋesiheɓeru naŋesiroma naŋesiɡreki ɓase ɓetʰi aɓapristi aɓakʰulu ɓaɓad͡ʒuda kupilatu uŋaloɓi ukutʰi ‘iŋkosi jaɓad͡ʒuda kepʰa ukuɓa jena watʰi ‘ŋijiŋkosi jaɓad͡ʒuda upilatu wapʰendula watʰi eŋikuloɓile ŋikuloɓile kutʰe amaɓutʰo esembetʰele ud͡ʒesu esipʰambanweni atʰatʰa iziŋuɓo zakʰe izaɓelo kwaɓa jilelo ɓutʰo laɓa nesaɓelo nejembe futʰi kepʰa ijembe laliŋenamtʰuŋo loŋke pʰezulu ŋakʰoke akʰuluma atʰi asiŋalidaɓuli iŋkatʰo jokutʰi lijakuɓa ŋelikaɓani kuɡǀ̤waliseke otʰi ɓaɓelana iziŋuɓo ɓenzelana iŋkatʰo ŋesambatʰo lokʰoke amaɓutʰo kepʰa ŋasesipʰambanweni sikad͡ʒesu kaɲe nodadewaɓo umarija umkakxejopʰase nomarija maɡdalena kutʰe ud͡ʒesu eɓona amtʰandajo ɓemi ŋakʰona watʰi mame beka jakʰo wajesetʰi beka uɲoko kusukela sikʰatʰi wamjisa kwakʰe emva kwalokʰo ud͡ʒesu ukutʰi koŋke sekupʰelelisiwe ukuɓa uɡǀ̤waliseke watʰi ŋomile kwakuɓekiwe kʰona isit͡ʃa siɡǀ̤wele uviniɡa kʰona ɓaǀʰoma liɡǀ̤wele uviniɡa otʰini ɓalijisa emloɲeni wakʰe kwatʰi ukuɓa ud͡ʒesu uviniɡa watʰi kufeziwe waɡeɓisa ikʰanda kʰona aɓad͡ʒuda ŋokuɓa kwakuŋolokuluŋisela ziŋaɬali esipʰambanweni ŋesaɓatʰa ŋokuɓa lwesaɓatʰa lwalulukʰulu ɓaŋǁusa upilatu ukuɓa japʰulwe jaɓo ɓasuswe ajesezake amaɓutʰo ajapʰula jowokuǃala nejomuɲe owajeɓetʰelwe naje esefika kud͡ʒesu eɓona ukutʰi kawajapʰulaŋa jakʰe eliɲe lamaɓutʰo lamɡwaza oɬaŋotʰini ŋomkʰonto kwapʰuma masiɲane iɡazi oɓonilejo uɓufakazi ɓakʰe ɓuǃinisile jenake ujazi ukutʰi ukʰuluma iǃiniso nikʰolwe ŋokuɓa lokʰo ukuɓa kuɡǀ̤waliseke otʰi akujikwapʰulwa tʰambo lakʰe futʰi omuɲe utʰi ɓajakumbheka aɓamɡwazilejo emva kwalokʰo ud͡ʒosefa wasearimatʰeja eŋumfundi kad͡ʒesu kepʰa ekufiɬa ŋokwesaɓa aɓad͡ʒuda waǀela kupilatu ukuɓa sikad͡ʒesu upilatu wajesefika sikad͡ʒesu kweza nonikodemu kuje kuǃala eɓusuku waletʰa iǁuɓe lenɬaka nomɬaɓa kuŋatʰi ajikʰulu ŋakʰo ɓase ɓesitʰatʰa sikad͡ʒesu ɓasisoŋa ŋezindwaŋu kaɲe namakʰa ɲd͡ʒeŋesiko laɓad͡ʒuda kʰona ŋakulejo lapʰo wajeɓetʰelwe kʰona esipʰambanweni kwakukʰona kukʰona itʰuna eliʃa okwakuŋazaŋe kuɓekwe ɓambeka lapʰoke ud͡ʒesu ŋeŋǁa jolokuluŋisela lwaɓad͡ʒuda ŋokuɓa ɓejiɓeke kʰona ŋakʰo wajesepʰuma upetru nomuɲe ɓeza etʰuneni ɓaɡid͡ʒima ɓoɓaɓili kaɲekaɲe kepʰa omuɲe waɡid͡ʒima kakʰulu kunopetru kuǃala etʰuneni eluŋuza waɓona izindwaŋu zikʰona kepʰa akaŋenaŋa kʰona nosimoni petru waŋena etʰuneni waɓona izindwaŋu zikʰona eɓelisekʰanda lakʰe liɓekiwe liŋekʰo ezindwaŋwini kepʰa lisoŋwe kweɲe kʰona wajeseŋena omuɲe kuǃala etʰuneni waɓona wakʰolwa ŋokuɓa wapʰenduka watʰi kuje ŋesiheɓeru raɓuni okuŋukutʰi mfundisi ud͡ʒesu watʰi kuje uŋaŋitʰinti ŋokuɓa aŋikeɲukeli kuɓaɓa kepʰa jana kuɓazalwane ɓami uɓat͡ʃele ukutʰi ŋeɲukela kuɓaɓa nojiɬo kuŋkuluŋkulu noŋkuluŋkulu umarija maɡdalena waɓikela aɓafundi ukutʰi ŋijiɓonile iŋkosi nokutʰi iʃilo lokʰo kwatʰike kusiɬwa ŋalolo olokuǃala imiɲaŋo lapʰo aɓafundi ɓekʰona ŋokwesaɓa aɓad͡ʒuda ud͡ʒesu pʰakatʰi kwaɓo watʰi kuɓo ukutʰula makuɓe eseʃilo lokʰo waɓakʰombisa izanɮa noɬaŋotʰi lwakʰe ɓase ɓetʰokoza aɓafundi ɓejiɓona iŋkosi kʰona ud͡ʒesu waɓuje watʰi kuɓo ukutʰula makuɓe ɲd͡ʒeŋokuɓa uɓaɓa eŋitʰume ŋoŋakʰolwajo okʰolwajo utomase wapʰendula watʰi kuje ŋkosi jami ŋkuluŋkulu ud͡ʒesu watʰi kuje ŋokuɓa uŋiɓonile ukʰoliwe ɓaɓusisiwe aɓakʰolwa ɓeŋaɓonaŋa iziɓonakaliso eziɲe eziniŋi ud͡ʒesu pʰambi waziɓonakalisa kuɓafundi ŋaselwanɮe lwasetiɓerija waziɓonakalisa kaɲd͡ʒe kwakukʰona ndawoɲe osimoni petru notomase otʰiwa udidimu nonatʰanajeli wasekʰana laseɡalile naɓakazeɓedewu naɓaɲe aɓaɓili ŋud͡ʒesu ud͡ʒesu watʰike kuɓo ɓantwana aninakʰo ukuɮa ɓampʰendula ɓatʰi ǃʰa wajesetʰi kuɓo pʰonsani inetʰa ŋakwesokunene somkʰumbi nizakutʰola ɓase ɓepʰonsa aɓaɓe ɓesaɓa namanɮa ŋeŋǁa joɓuniŋi ɓezinɬanzi kʰona ud͡ʒesu amtʰandajo watʰi kupetru jiŋkosi usimoni petru ukutʰi jiŋkosi waɡǃ̤oka ŋokuɓa wajehamba wazipʰonsa elwanɮe kepʰa aɓaɲe aɓafundi ɓeza ŋesikebe ŋokuɓa ɓeɓeŋekude nenɬaɓatʰi maɲd͡ʒe wasuka usimoni petru emɬaɓatʰini inetʰa liɡǀ̤wele izinɬanzi eziŋkulu zijikʰulu namaʃumi ajisiɬanu nantatʰu ziŋako inetʰa alidaɓukaŋa ud͡ʒesu watʰi kuɓo wozani niɮe kepʰa akwaɓakʰo kuɓafundi owaɓa nesiɓindi ŋokutʰi uŋuɓani ɓazi ukutʰi jijo iŋkosi ud͡ʒesu watʰaɓatʰa isiŋkwa waɓapʰa nezinɬanzi futʰi lokʰo sekuŋokwesitʰatʰu ud͡ʒesu eɓonakaliswa kuɓafundi kwaɓafilejo kʰona seɓeɮile ud͡ʒesu watʰi kusimoni petru simoni kad͡ʒona ujaŋitʰanda kunalaɓa watʰi kuje jeɓo ŋkosi ujazi ukutʰi ŋijakutʰanda watʰi kuje jipʰa amawunɮu waɓuje watʰi kuje ŋokwesiɓili simoni kad͡ʒona ujaŋitʰanda watʰi kuje ukutʰi ŋijakutʰanda ud͡ʒesu watʰi kuje jipʰa ŋiǃinisile ŋiǃinisile ŋitʰi usemuʃa wawuɡǃ̤oka lapʰo utʰanda kʰona kepʰa ŋǁa ujakwelula izanɮa zakʰo omuɲe akuɡǃ̤okise akujise lapʰo uŋatʰandi kʰona kepʰa wakuʃo lokʰo ekʰomba uŋkuluŋkulu ŋakʰo eseʃilo lokʰo watʰi ŋilandele upetru epʰenduka waɓona ud͡ʒesu amtʰandajo ojena futʰi wajeŋǀike esifuɓeni sakʰe ekuɮeni nowatʰi ŋkosi ŋuɓani ozakukukʰapʰela kutʰe upetru watʰi kud͡ʒesu ŋkosi kepʰa pʰo ud͡ʒesu watʰi kuje uma ŋitʰanda ukuɓa aɬale ŋize ŋifike kujini wena ŋakʰoke lapʰumela kuɓazalwane lokutʰi akajikufa kanti ud͡ʒesu akaʃoŋo ukutʰi akajikufa ukutʰi uma ŋitʰanda ukuɓa aɬale ŋize ŋifike kujini ŋuje ŋalezi nokuloɓile lokʰu sijazi ukutʰi uɓufakazi ɓakʰe ɓuǃinisile kukʰona neziɲe eziniŋi ud͡ʒesu zilot͡ʃiwe ŋaziɲe ŋitʰi loŋke liŋezanele iziŋǀwadi eziŋalot͡ʃwa iŋǀwadi jokuǃala ŋajiloɓa tʰejofilu ŋakʰo koŋke ud͡ʒesu aǃala kwaɓa akʰuʃulwa ŋalo eseɓajalile ŋomoja oŋǀ̤wele aɓapʰostoli ajeɓakʰetʰile kuɓo epʰilile kokuɬupʰeka kwakʰe ŋoɓufakazi oɓuniŋi waɓonwa jiɓo eziŋamaʃumi ekʰuluma ŋezombuso kaŋkuluŋkulu kwatʰi eɬaŋene naɓo waɓajala ŋokutʰi niŋamuki ed͡ʒerusalema niɬalele isitʰembiso sikajise ŋami ŋokuɓa ud͡ʒohane wajebapatʰiza ŋamanzi kepʰa nizakubapatʰizwa ŋomoja oŋǀ̤wele kuŋakaɮuli eziniŋi kʰona laɓo aɓaɓeɓutʰene ɓambuza ɓatʰi ŋkosi usawuɓujisela kuisrajeli ŋalesi sikʰatʰi watʰi kuɓo akusikʰo izikʰatʰi uɓaɓa ŋamanɮa akʰe amanɮa umoja oŋǀ̤wele pʰezu niɓe ŋofakazi ɓami ed͡ʒerusalema nased͡ʒudija loŋke nasesamarija kuɓe sekuɡǀ̤ineni komɬaɓa kwatʰi eseʃilo lokʰo wakʰuʃulwa ɓeɓuka emeɬweni aɓo ɓatʰi ɓesaɡǃ̤olozela beka amaɓili ajemi kuɓo embetʰe iziŋuɓo ezimɬopʰe atʰi madoda aseɡalile nibeka ud͡ʒesu eɲuselwa ujakuza kaɲd͡ʒalo ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰo eja kʰona ɓaɓujela ed͡ʒerusalema ɓevela entaɓeni etʰiwa ejemiŋǃumo ned͡ʒerusalema iɓaŋa lwesaɓatʰa kwatʰi seɓeŋenile ɓeɲukela elipʰezulu lapʰo ɓeɓeɬala kʰona opetru nod͡ʒohane nod͡ʒakoɓe noandreja nofilipʰu notomase noɓartolomewu nomatʰewu nod͡ʒakoɓe kaalfewu nosimoni umzelotʰe nod͡ʒuda kad͡ʒakoɓe ɓoŋke laɓa ɓaǃinisela ŋanɬizijoɲe ekukʰulekeni kaɲe naɓesifazane nomarija kad͡ʒesu naɓafowaɓo ŋalejo miɬa upetru pʰakatʰi kwaɓazalwane isiǁuku saɓantu esasikʰona ndawoɲe kwakuŋatʰi ikʰulu namaʃumi amaɓili watʰi madoda ɓazalwane ukuɓa kuɡǀ̤waliseke umoja oŋǀ̤wele awukʰulumajo ŋapʰambili ŋomlomo kadavide ŋod͡ʒuda owajeŋumholi kulaɓo aɓaɓamba ud͡ʒesu ŋokuɓa wajeɓalwe kaɲe natʰi watʰola isaɓelo ŋkonzo lowoke ŋomvuzo wokuŋaluŋi ŋekʰanda waǃʰuma pʰakatʰi neziɓilini zakʰe zoŋke zaǀʰitʰeka jiɓo ɓoŋke aɓakʰilejo ed͡ʒerusalema jaze jaǃaɲd͡ʒwa lejo ŋolimi lwakuɓo ŋokutʰi iakeldama okuŋukutʰi insimu jeɡazi ŋokuɓa kulot͡ʃiwe eŋǀwadini jamahuɓo ukutʰi umuzi wakʰe mawuɓe jiɬane kuŋaɓikʰo oɬala nokutʰi isikʰunɮa sakʰe asitʰatʰwe ŋomuɲe ŋakʰo ajehamba natʰi isikʰatʰi soŋke lapʰo iŋkosi ud͡ʒesu iŋena ipʰuma pʰakatʰi kwetʰu kuǃalela embhapatʰizweni kad͡ʒohane kwaɓa akʰuʃulwa ŋalo kitʰi ukuɓa eɲe iɓe ŋufakazi kaɲe natʰi ŋokuvuka kwakʰe ɓase ɓemisa aɓaɓili ud͡ʒosefa otʰiwa uɓarsaɓa otʰiwa futʰi ud͡ʒustu kaɲe nomatʰija ɓase ɓekʰuleka ɓetʰi wena ŋkosi izinɬizijo zaɓantu ɓoŋke ukʰombe omuɲe kulaɓa aɓaɓili omkʰetʰilejo ukuɓa atʰatʰe isikʰunɮa ŋkonzo noɓupʰostoli apʰambuka ud͡ʒuda ukuja jakʰe ɓase ɓeɓenzela iŋkatʰo jaɮa umatʰija waɓalwa kaɲe naɓapʰostoli aɓajiʃumi naɲe kwatʰi lwepʰentekoste ɓoŋke ɓaɓeɓutʰene ndawoɲe ŋokuŋazelelwe inɬokomo kwaŋatʰi ejokuvuŋuza komoja onamanɮa jona jaɡǀ̤walisa inɮu joŋke aɓaɓeɬezi kujo kwase kuɓonakala kuɓo ezaɬukenejo kuŋatʰi zaɬala pʰezu kuɓo ɓase ɓeɡǀ̤wala ɓoŋke umoja oŋǀ̤wele ɓaǃala ukukʰuluma ŋeziɲe ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰo umoja waɓapʰa ukupʰumisela kepʰa kwakukʰona aɓad͡ʒuda aɓakʰile ed͡ʒerusalema akʰolwajo zoŋke ezipʰansi kwatʰi uǃuǃaɓa lwaɓutʰana lwapʰitʰiza ŋokuɓa kwaɓa jilowo waɓezwa ɓekʰuluma ŋolimi lwakuɓo ɓetʰuka ɓamaŋala ɓatʰi beka ɓoŋke laɓa aɓakʰulumajo aɓasiɓo aɓaseɡalile jini pʰo ukuɓa soŋke ŋaɓaɲe ŋolimi lwakitʰi amaparte namamede namaelamitʰi naɓakʰile emesopotamija nased͡ʒudija nasekʰapʰadosija nasepontu naseasija nasefriɡija nasepʰamfilija naseɡiɓitʰe laseliɓija ŋasekʰurene zaseroma naɓad͡ʒuda aɓasekretʰe naɓasearaɓija sijaɓezwa ɓekʰuluma ŋezilimi zakitʰi ŋemiseɓenzi emikʰulu kaŋkuluŋkulu ɓoŋke ɓamaŋala ɓasambatʰeka ɓatʰi omuɲe komuɲe kutʰini lokʰu kepʰa aɓaɲe ɓeɓabuǃa ɓatʰi ɓaɡǀ̤wele iwajini wajesesukuma upetru naɓajiʃumi naɲe wapʰakamisa lakʰe wapʰumisela watʰi kuɓo madoda akwad͡ʒuda noŋke enakʰilejo ed͡ʒerusalema lokʰu niɓeke inɮeɓe ŋokuɓa laɓa kaɓadakiwe ɲd͡ʒeŋokuǀaɓaŋa lokʰu kusejihora lesitʰatʰu lokʰu kujikʰo okwakʰuluɲwa ŋomprofetʰi ud͡ʒoweli ukutʰi ‘kujakutʰi zokupʰela kuʃo uŋkuluŋkulu ŋijakutʰulula umoja pʰezu kwajo joŋke iɲama ajakuprofetʰa ziɓone imiɓono aɓadala ɓenu ɓapʰupʰe amapʰupʰo jeɓo napʰezu kweziŋǀeku neziŋǀekukazi ŋijakutʰulula umoja ŋalejo miɬa zijakuprofetʰa ŋijakuveza izimaŋaliso pʰezulu neziɓonakaliso emɬaɓeni pʰansi iɡazi nokutʰuŋǃa ilaŋa lijakupʰenduka uɓumɲama iɲaŋa iɓe jiɡazi luŋakafiki olukʰulu noluǃʰamilejo lweŋkosi kujakutʰi jilowo oɓiza iɡama leŋkosi ujakusindiswa madoda akwaisrajeli ud͡ʒesu wasenazaretʰa ŋuŋkuluŋkulu pʰambi ŋemiseɓenzi jamanɮa naŋezimaŋaliso naŋeziɓonakaliso uŋkuluŋkulu ŋaje pʰakatʰi ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰu uǃoɓo jena ŋesu elimisiwejo naŋokwazipʰambili kukaŋkuluŋkulu nambetʰela ŋezanɮa zaɓaŋenamtʰetʰo uŋkuluŋkulu etʰukulula imiɲd͡ʒuɲd͡ʒu jokufa lokʰu kwakuŋenakwenzeka ukuɓa aɓaɲd͡ʒwe jikʰo ŋokuɓa udavide utʰi ŋaje ‘ŋajiɓona iŋkosi pʰambi ɲd͡ʒalo ŋokuɓa iŋakwesokunene ŋiŋaɲakaziswa ŋalokʰo inɬizijo jami ijad͡ʒaɓula lujetʰaɓa ŋiʃo neɲama jami ijakuɬala ŋokwetʰemba ŋokuɓa awujikuʃija umpʰefumulo ehajidese futʰi awujikuvuma oŋǀ̤wele wakʰo aɓone ukuɓola waŋazisa izinɮela zokupʰila ujakuŋiɡǀ̤walisa ŋokud͡ʒaɓula eɓusweni ɓakʰo madoda ɓazalwane ŋikʰulume ŋokusoɓala ŋokʰokʰo udavide ukutʰi nokutʰi nokutʰi itʰuna lakʰe lisekʰona kitʰi nanamuɬa ŋakʰo lokʰu eŋumprofetʰi ukutʰi uŋkuluŋkulu wajefuŋile kuje ŋesifuŋo ukutʰi jokʰalo lwakʰe ujakuɓeka omuɲe esiɬalweni sakʰe soɓukʰosi eɓona pʰambili wakʰuluma ŋokuvuka kukakristu ukutʰi akaʃijwaŋa ehajidese neɲama jakʰe ajiɓonaŋa ukuɓola ud͡ʒesu uŋkuluŋkulu esiŋofakazi ɓakʰo tʰina soŋke ŋakʰo epʰakaɲiselwe ŋakwesokunene sikaŋkuluŋkulu kujise isitʰembiso sikamoja oŋǀ̤wele wakutʰulula lokʰu enikuɓonajo nenikuzwajo ŋokuɓa udavide akeɲukelaŋa kepʰa jena utʰi ‘iŋkosi jatʰi eŋkosini jami ɬala ŋakwesokunene ŋize ŋiɓeke izitʰa zakʰo ziɓe jisenaɓelo seziɲawo zakʰo ŋakʰo inɮu joŋke jakwaisrajeli majazi ukutʰi uŋkuluŋkulu iŋkosi nokristu ud͡ʒesu enambetʰela esipʰambanweni seɓekuzwa ɓaɬaɓeka enɬizijweni ɓatʰi kupetru nakwaɓaɲe aɓapʰostoli madoda ɓazalwane sijakwenze ɲd͡ʒani upetru wajesetʰi pʰendukani jilowo abapatʰizwe eɡameni likad͡ʒesu kristu kukʰo ukutʰetʰelelwa kʰona nijakwamukeliswa isipʰiwo sikamoja oŋǀ̤wele ŋokuɓa isitʰembiso ŋesenu nesaɓantwana ɓenu esaɓo ɓoŋke aɓakude ɓoŋke iŋkosi uŋkuluŋkulu wetʰu ejakuɓaɓiza wafakaza naŋamaɲe amaniŋi waɓajala watʰi zisindiseni esipʰambenejo ŋakʰo aɓalamukelejo lakʰe ɓabapatʰizwa ŋalowo muɬa aɓantu kuŋatʰi iziŋkuluŋwane ezintatʰu ɓaǃinisela ɲd͡ʒalo saɓapʰostoli nasekuɬaŋaneni nasekuɬepʰuleni isiŋkwa nasemikʰulekweni kepʰa kwaɓa jilowo weɬelwa ŋukwesaɓa ŋaɓapʰostoli izimaŋaliso neziɓonakaliso eziniŋi ɓoŋke aɓakʰolwajo ɓaɓe ndawoɲe ɓaɬaŋaɲela zoŋke ɓatʰeŋisa ŋemfujo naŋempaɬa ɓaɓela ɓoŋke ŋajo ɲd͡ʒeŋokuswela kwaɓo imiɬa ŋemiɬa ɓaǃinisela ŋanɬizijoɲe etʰempelini ɓaɬepʰula isiŋkwa ekʰaja ɓaɮa ukuɮa kwaɓo ŋentokozo naŋoɓumɬopʰe ɓenɬizijo ɓemdumisa uŋkuluŋkulu ɓetʰandeka kuɓantu ɓoŋke iŋkosi jenezela eɓanɮeni imiɬa ŋemiɬa aɓasindiswajo upetru nod͡ʒohane ɓakʰupʰukela etʰempelini ŋehora lokukʰuleka elesiʃijaɡaloluɲe kwase kuletʰwa etʰile ejisiʃoʃa aɓaɓejiɓeka imiɬa ŋemiɬa ŋasemɲaŋo wetʰempeli otʰiwa omuɬe ukuɓa iǀele ukwaɓelwa izipʰo kwaɓaŋenajo etʰempelini kwatʰi ukuɓa aɓone opetru nod͡ʒohane ɓezakuŋena etʰempelini waǀela ukwaɓelwa isipʰo kepʰa upetru wamɡǃ̤olozela kaɲe nod͡ʒohane watʰi sibeke wajeseɓabeka etʰemba ukuɓa utʰo kuɓo kodwa upetru watʰi isiliva neɡolide aŋinalo kepʰa lokʰo eŋinakʰo ŋikupʰa kʰona eɡameni likad͡ʒesu kristu wasenazaretʰa wajesembamba ŋesanɮa kwaǃina masiɲane iziɲawo zakʰe namaǃakala eɡǁ̤uma waŋena naɓo etʰempelini eɡǁ̤uma uŋkuluŋkulu aɓantu ɓoŋke ɓambona uŋkuluŋkulu kepʰa ɓase ɓemazi ukuɓa ŋujena owajeɬalela ukupʰiwa ŋasemɲaŋo omuɬe wetʰempeli ɓeɬelwa ŋukwesaɓa nokumaŋala ŋokwenzakele kuje esaɓambelele kopetru nod͡ʒohane ɓoŋke aɓantu ɓaɡid͡ʒimela kuɓo empʰemeni otʰiwa okasolomoni ɓesaɓa kakʰulu kʰona upetru eɓona lokʰo watʰatʰa watʰi kuɓantu madoda akwaisrajeli nimaŋalelani ŋalona nisiɡǃ̤olozelelani ŋokuŋatʰi ukuɓa ŋawetʰu amanɮa naŋokwetʰu ukukʰolwa uŋkuluŋkulu kaaɓrahama nokaisaka nokad͡ʒakoɓe uŋkuluŋkulu wawoɓaɓa ɓetʰu ujidumisile iŋǀeku jakʰe ud͡ʒesu enajikʰapʰela najipʰika eɓusweni ɓukapilatu jena eseŋǃumile ukujikʰulula kepʰa nampʰika oŋǀ̤wele noluŋilejo naǀela ukuɓa nipʰiwe oŋumbulali najiɓulala iŋkosi jokupʰila ajivusajo uŋkuluŋkulu kwaɓafilejo esiŋofakazi ɓakʰo tʰina ŋokukʰolwa eɡameni lajo enimbonajo nenimazijo iɡama lajo aǃine nokukʰolwa okuŋajo pʰambi noŋke kalokʰu ɓazalwane ŋijazi ukutʰi lokʰo ŋokuŋazi ɲd͡ʒeŋaɓo aɓaɓusi ɓenu kepʰa lokʰo uŋkuluŋkulu ŋapʰambili ŋomlomo waɓaprofetʰi ɓoŋke ukutʰi ukristu wakʰe ujakuɬupʰeka ukuɡǀ̤walisile kaɲd͡ʒe ŋalokʰu pʰendukani niɡuǃuke ukuɓa kuɬaŋulwe izikʰatʰi zokuɬuɲelelwa eɓusweni ɓeŋkosi nokuɓa itʰume ukristu d͡ʒesu enimmiselwejo ukuɓa kuɓe jizikʰatʰi zokuɓujiselwa kwakʰo koŋke uŋkuluŋkulu akʰuluma ŋakʰo ŋomlomo waɓaprofetʰi ɓakʰe aɓaŋǀ̤wele kwapʰakade umose watʰi ‘iŋkosi uŋkuluŋkulu ijakunivusela umprofetʰi kuɓazalwane ɓenu ɲd͡ʒeŋami nijakumlalela kukʰo koŋke azakukukʰuluma kujakutʰi woŋke oŋajikumlalela mprofetʰi ujakuǀʰitʰwa kuɓantu jeɓo naɓaprofetʰi ɓoŋke kusamuweli naɓalandelajo ɓoŋke aɓakʰulumilejo ɓamemezela nina niŋamadodana aɓaprofetʰi uŋkuluŋkulu asenzajo nawojiɬo etʰi kuaɓrahama ‘ŋenzalo jakʰo ijakuɓusiswa joŋke jomɬaɓa uŋkuluŋkulu esejivusile iŋǀeku jakʰe wajitʰumela kuǃala ukuniɓusisa ŋokuniɡuǃula kuɓe jilowo eɓuɓini ɓakʰe kepʰa ɓesakʰuluma kuɓantu aɓapristi jetʰempeli naɓasadusi ɓaɓafikela ɓeneŋwa ŋukufundisa kwaɓo aɓantu ŋod͡ʒesu kwaɓafilejo ɓaɓaɓamba ɓaɓafaka etiloŋweni kwaɓa ŋokuɓa kuɬwile kepʰa aɓaniŋi kwaɓezwajo ɓakʰolwa waɓa kuŋatʰi iziŋkuluŋwane ezijisiɬanu kwatʰi ŋaŋomuso kwaɓutʰana ed͡ʒerusalema aɓaɓusi namaluŋa naɓabali ɓaɓo noanase omkʰulu nokajafase nod͡ʒohane noaleksandru naɓo ɓoŋke aɓenɮu jompristi omkʰulu ɓaɓamisa pʰakatʰi kwaɓo ɓaɓaɓuza ɓatʰi lokʰo ŋamapʰi amanɮa naŋalipʰi iɡama kʰona upetru eɡǀ̤wele umoja oŋǀ̤wele watʰi kuɓo nina ɓaɓusi ɓezizwe namaluŋa ŋǁa siɓuzwa namuɬa ŋomseɓenzi omuɬe oɡulajo ukutʰi jena ŋani noŋke soŋke sakwaisrajeli ukutʰi ŋeɡama likad͡ʒesu kristu wasenazaretʰa enambetʰela esipʰambanweni amvusajo uŋkuluŋkulu kwaɓafilejo ŋaje pʰambi jena ujit͡ʃe jinina ɓakʰi eselaɓa jinɬoko jeɡumbi ajikʰo ŋomuɲe ŋokuɓa alikʰo futʰi eliɲe iɡama pʰansi eɓantwini ŋalo kwatʰi ɓeɓona isiɓindi sikapetru nod͡ʒohane ɓeǃonda ukutʰi ɓaŋaɓantu aɓaŋafundile ɓajimifunda ɲd͡ʒe ɓamaŋala ɓaɓazi ukutʰi ɓenod͡ʒesu kepʰa ɓeɓona opʰilisiwejo naɓo ɓaɓeŋenakupʰika lutʰo kodwa seɓeɓajalile ukuɓa ɓapʰume empʰakatʰini ɓalulekana ɓodwa ɓatʰi sizakuɓenzani laɓa ɓantu ŋokuɓa kusoɓala kuɓo ɓoŋke aɓakʰilejo ed͡ʒerusalema ukutʰi isiɓonakaliso esiǃʰamilejo jiɓo asinakukupʰika kodwa kuŋaɓe pʰakatʰi kwaɓantu asiɓalaje ɓaŋaɓe ɓesakʰuluma namuɲe ŋalelo ɡama ɓase ɓeɓaɓiza ɓaɓajala ŋokutʰi ɓaŋakʰulumi ɓaŋafundisi nakaɲe ŋeɡama likad͡ʒesu kepʰa opetru nod͡ʒohane ɓapʰendula ɓatʰi kuɓo ŋǃumani ukuɓa kuluŋile jini eɓusweni ɓukaŋkuluŋkulu kunoŋkuluŋkulu ŋokuɓa tʰina asinakujeka ukukʰuluma ŋalokʰo esikuɓonilejo nesikuzwilejo kʰona seɓeɓalajile futʰi ɓaɓajeka ɓeŋafumanaŋa ukutʰi ɓaŋaɓad͡ʒezisa kaɲd͡ʒani ŋeŋǁa jaɓantu ŋokuɓa ɓoŋke ɓedumisa uŋkuluŋkulu ŋalokʰo okwenzekilejo ŋokuɓa kuje siɓonakaliso sokupʰulukiswa wajenemiɲaka emaʃumini seɓejekiwe ɓaja kwaɓakuɓo ɓaɓika koŋke aɓapristi aɓakʰulu namaluŋa aɓekuʃilo kuɓo ɓona seɓezwile ɓapʰakamisa kuŋkuluŋkulu ŋanɬizijoɲe ɓatʰi somanɮa nomɬaɓa nolwanɮe nakʰo koŋke okukukʰo owaʃo ŋomoja oŋǀ̤wele ŋomlomo kaɓaɓa udavide iŋǀeku jakʰo ukutʰi ‘kuŋani ukuɓa aɓezizwe ɓaǁokozele naɓantu ɓaǀeɓe okujize amakʰosi omɬaɓa aǃʰelile naɓaɓusi ɓajiɬaŋaɲele iŋkosi noɡǀ̤ot͡ʃiwejo wajo ŋokuɓa ŋempela oherode nopontiju pilatu kaɲe naɓezizwe naɓantu ɓakwaisrajeli ɓajiɬaŋaɲela iŋǀeku jakʰo ukupʰulukisa iziɓonakaliso nezimaŋaliso ŋeɡama leŋǀeku jakʰo eŋǀ̤wele ud͡ʒesu kwatʰi seɓekʰulekile kwazaɲazaɲiswa lapʰo ɓeɓeɓutʰene kʰona ɓaɡǀ̤waliswa ɓoŋke ŋumoja oŋǀ̤wele ɓakʰuluma likaŋkuluŋkulu ŋesiɓindi isiǁuku saɓakʰolwajo sasinɬizijoɲe nompʰefumulo muɲe akwaɓakʰo nojedwa owaʃo ŋezimpaɬa zakʰe ukutʰi ŋezakʰe ɓakuɬaŋaɲela koŋke aɓapʰostoli ɓaveza ŋamanɮa amakʰulu uɓufakazi ŋokuvuka kweŋkosi ud͡ʒesu omkʰulu wawupʰezu kwaɓo ɓoŋke kwakuŋekʰo oswelajo pʰakatʰi kwaɓo ŋokuɓa ɓoŋke aɓaɓeŋaɓanikazi ɓamazwe ɓezinɮu ɓatʰeŋisa ŋakʰo ɓaletʰa jalokʰo aɓatʰeŋise ŋakʰo ɓajiɓeka ŋaseziɲaweni ajisikʰombisa nanɬanu ud͡ʒakoɓe weɬela eɡiɓitʰe jena nawoɓaɓa ɓajiswa esikemi ɓaɓekwa etʰuneni alitʰeŋa uaɓrahama ŋenani kahamori esikemi kepʰa isikʰatʰi sesitʰembiso uŋkuluŋkulu asiʃo kuaɓrahama ɓanda aɓantu ɓaɓa ɓaniŋi eɡiɓitʰe eɲe iŋkosi eɡiɓitʰe eɓiŋamazi ud͡ʒosefa jona jasipʰatʰa ŋoɓuǃili sakitʰi jaɓaɬupʰa oɓaɓa ŋokuɓalaɬisa iziŋane zaɓo ziŋapʰili ŋaleso sikʰatʰi umose waɓa muɬe uŋkuluŋkulu uɓanika ŋesanɮa sakʰe kepʰa aɓakuǃondaŋa naŋaŋomuso kuɓo ɓelwa ukuɓalamula ɓaɓujisane watʰi ‘madoda niŋaɓazalwane nipʰatʰanelani kaɓi kepʰa owajemona umakʰelwane wakʰe wamɬoɬoloza watʰi ‘uɓekwe ŋuɓani uɓe ŋumbusi nomaɬuleli pʰezu kwetʰu usufuna ukuŋiɓulala ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰo uɓulele owaseɡiɓitʰe kʰona umose waɓaleka ŋeŋǁa jalelo waɓa ŋumfokazi lakwamidijani lapʰo kʰona amaɓili kwatʰi sekupʰelele imiɲaka eŋamaʃumi kwaɓonakala kuje eɬane lentaɓa jasesinaji iŋelosi iselaŋaɓini esiɬaɬeni umose ekuɓona wamaŋala ŋalowo ukuɓa abekisise leŋkosi latʰi ‘ŋiŋuŋkuluŋkulu wawojiɬo uŋkuluŋkulu kaaɓrahama nokaisaka nokad͡ʒakoɓe umose watʰutʰumela akaɓa nasiɓindi sokubekisisa iŋkosi jajisitʰi kuje ‘kʰumula iziǀatʰulo eziɲaweni zakʰo ŋokuɓa kujo iŋumɬaɓatʰi oŋǀ̤wele ŋikuɓonile nokukuɓona ukuɬuʃwa esiseɡiɓitʰe ŋizwile ukuɓuɓula seŋeɬile ukuɓa ŋiɓakʰipʰe woza kalokʰu ŋizakukutʰumela eɡiɓitʰe umose aɓamalajo ɓetʰi ‘uɓekwe ŋuɓani uɓe ŋumbusi nomaɬuleli ŋujena amtʰumajo uŋkuluŋkulu ŋesanɮa seŋelosi ejaɓonakala kuje esiɬaɬeni aɓe ŋumbusi nomɬeŋi jena waɓakʰipʰa izimaŋaliso neziɓonakaliso laseɡiɓitʰe naselwanɮe oluɓomvu naseɬane imiɲaka eŋamaʃumi ŋuje umose owatʰi kuɓantwana ɓakwaisrajeli ‘uŋkuluŋkulu ujakunivusela umprofetʰi kuɓafowenu oɲd͡ʒeŋami ŋuje owajeseɓanɮeni eɬane kaɲe neŋelosi ejakʰuluma naje entaɓeni jasesinaji kaɲe nawoɓaɓa okupʰila kepʰa oɓaɓa aɓavumaŋa ɓamɬoɬoloza ɓaɓujela eɡiɓitʰe ŋezinɬizijo zaɓo ɓatʰi kuaroni ‘senzele oŋkuluŋkulu aɓazakuhamba pʰambi kwetʰu ŋokuɓa umose owasikʰipʰa laseɡiɓitʰe ukuɓa weɬelwe jini ɓenza itʰole ŋalejo miɬa ɓaletʰa umɬat͡ʃelo esitʰombeni ɓad͡ʒaɓula ŋemiseɓenzi jezanɮa zaɓo kepʰa uŋkuluŋkulu waɓafulatʰela waɓadedela ukuɓa ɓakʰonze iɓanɮa ɲd͡ʒeŋokuɓa kulot͡ʃiwe eŋǀwadini jaɓaprofetʰi ukutʰi ‘naniŋiletʰela nemiɬat͡ʃelo imiɲaka eŋamaʃumi eɬane nɮu kaisrajeli ǃʰa natʰatʰa likamoloki neŋkaɲezi kaŋkuluŋkulu uremfani enajenza ukuɓa nikʰuleke kujo ŋijakunimukisela ŋapʰambili kweɓaɓiloni kwakukʰona loɓufakazi koɓaɓa eɬane ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰo akujalajo jena owakʰuluma nomose ukuɓa ŋomfanekiso aɓewuɓonile oɓaɓa ɓenod͡ʒoʃuwa ɓalamukela ɓaliŋenisa aziǁoʃajo uŋkuluŋkulu eɓusweni ɓawoɓaɓa kwaɓa semiɬeni kadavide owatʰola eɓusweni ɓukaŋkuluŋkulu waǀela uŋkuluŋkulu kad͡ʒakoɓe kepʰa ŋusolomoni owamakʰela inɮu kodwa opʰezukoŋke akaɬali ezinɮini ŋezanɮa ɲd͡ʒeŋokuʃo komprofetʰi ukutʰi ‘izulu lijisiɬalo soɓukʰosi nomɬaɓa ujisenaɓelo seziɲawo ŋeɲd͡ʒani inɮu enijakuŋakʰela jona iʃo iŋkosi jijipʰi jami jokupʰumula isanɮa asikwenzaŋa koŋke lokʰo nina ɓantamo zilukʰuni aɓaŋasokile ezinɬizijweni nasezinɮeɓeni ɲd͡ʒalo nomoja oŋǀ̤wele ɲd͡ʒeŋojiɬo niɲd͡ʒalo ŋumupʰi kuɓaprofetʰi ojiɬo aɓaŋamziŋelaŋa ɓaɓaɓulala aɓaɓememezela ŋapʰambili koluŋilejo eseniŋaɓakʰapʰeli naɓaɓulali ɓakʰe umtʰetʰo ŋokujala kweziŋelosi kepʰa aniwuɡǀ̤inaŋa kwatʰi ɓekuzwa lokʰo ɓaɬaɓeka ezinɬizijweni ɓamɡuɡudela amaziɲo kepʰa jena eɡǀ̤wele umoja oŋǀ̤wele waɡǃ̤olozela waɓona iŋkazimulo kaŋkuluŋkulu nod͡ʒesu ŋakwesokunene sikaŋkuluŋkulu watʰi beka ŋiɓona nendodana jomuntu ŋakwesokunene sikaŋkuluŋkulu ɓase ɓekʰamuluka ŋezwi elikʰulu ɓavala izinɮeɓe ɓatʰeleka kuje kaɲekaɲe ɓamkʰipʰela ŋapʰanɮe ɓamkʰanda ŋamat͡ʃe ofakazi ɓaɓeka iziŋuɓo zaɓo ŋaseziɲaweni eɡama lajo liŋusawulu ustefanu ɓamkʰanda ŋamat͡ʃe ekʰuleka etʰi ŋkosi d͡ʒesu jamukela umoja wajeseɡuǃa pʰansi ŋezwi elikʰulu watʰi ŋkosi uŋaɓaɓaleli eseʃilo lokʰo uɓutʰoŋo kepʰa usawulu wajevumelene naɓo ŋokuɓulawa kwakʰe ŋalolo ukuziŋelwa okukʰulu kweɓanɮa lased͡ʒerusalema ɓaɬakazeka ɓoŋke ased͡ʒudija nasesamarija aɓapʰostoli ɓodwa amadoda akʰolwajo ustefanu amkʰalela esikʰulu kepʰa usawulu waliǀʰitʰa iɓanɮa eŋena ezinɮini ŋezinɮu aɓesilisa naɓesifazane waɓafaka etiloŋweni aɓaɬakazekilejo ɓase ɓehamba ɓeʃumajela levaŋeli ufilipʰu weɬela wasesamarija waɓaʃumajeza ukristu iziǁuku ŋanɬizijoɲe okwakʰuluɲwa ŋufilipʰu ziɓona iziɓonakaliso azenzajo ŋokuɓa kwapʰuma omoja aɓaŋǀ̤olilejo kwaɓaniŋi aɓakʰwelwa jiɓo ɓememeza ŋezwi elikʰulu naɓaniŋi aɓafe uɬaŋotʰi naɓajiziɲoŋa ɓapʰulukiswa kwaɓa kʰona ukutʰokoza okukʰulu kepʰa kwakukʰona etʰile ŋusimoni iɡama lajo ejajikade jenza imiliŋo isimaŋalisa sasesamarija iziʃaja omkʰulu ɓanamatʰela kuje ɓoŋke kwaɓaŋǀiɲane kuɓe kwaɓakʰulu ɓetʰi lo uŋamanɮa kaŋkuluŋkulu aɓizwa ŋokutʰi makʰulu ɓaɓenamatʰela kuje ŋokuɓa eɓamaŋalisile isikʰatʰi ŋemiliŋo jakʰe kepʰa ɓatʰi ukuɓa ɓakʰolwe ŋufilipʰu eʃumajela ivaŋeli ŋombuso kaŋkuluŋkulu naŋeɡama likad͡ʒesu kristu ɓabapatʰizwa aɓesilisa naɓesifazane naje usimoni wakʰolwa watʰi esebapatʰiziwe wanamatʰela kufilipʰu wamaŋala eɓona iziɓonakaliso nemiseɓenzi emikʰulu jamanɮa ejenziwajo kwatʰi ukuɓa aɓapʰostoli ɓased͡ʒerusalema ɓezwe ukutʰi isamarija likaŋkuluŋkulu ɓatʰumela kuɓo opetru nod͡ʒohane seɓeɬele kʰona ɓaɓakʰulekela ukuɓa ɓamukele umoja oŋǀ̤wele ŋokuɓa wajeŋakeɬeli nakojedwa kuɓo ɓaɓesabapatʰiziwe eɡameni leŋkosi ud͡ʒesu kupʰela kʰona ɓaɓeka izanɮa pʰezu kwaɓo ɓase ɓamukelake umoja oŋǀ̤wele kepʰa usimoni eɓonile ukutʰi ŋokuɓekwa kwezanɮa zaɓapʰostoli ujapʰiwa umoja waletʰa kuɓo watʰi ŋipʰeni manɮa jilowo eŋiɓeka izanɮa pʰezu kwakʰe umoja oŋǀ̤wele kepʰa upetru watʰi kuje isiliva lakʰo malibube kaɲe ŋokuɓa utʰi isipʰo sikaŋkuluŋkulu siŋatʰeŋwa ŋemali awunasaɓelo ŋokuɓa inɬizijo jakʰo ajiluŋile pʰambi kukaŋkuluŋkulu ŋakʰoke pʰenduka kuloɓu ɓuɓi ɓakʰo uŋǁuse eŋkosini iŋaɓe uŋatʰetʰelelwa jini isizinɮo senɬizijo jakʰo ŋokuɓa ŋijaɓona ukutʰi useɲoŋweni eɓaɓajo nasekuɓoʃweni kokuɓi usimoni wajesepʰendula etʰi ŋiŋǁuseleni eŋkosini kuŋeɬeli lutʰo lwalokʰo enikuʃilojo kutʰe seɓefakazile ɓelikʰulumile leŋkosi ɓaɓujela ed͡ʒerusalema ɓaʃumajela ivaŋeli eminiŋi jaɓasesamarija kepʰa iŋelosi jeŋkosi jakʰuluma kufilipʰu jatʰi suka uje ŋaseniŋizimu enɮeleni epʰuma ed͡ʒerusalema eɬela eɡaza jona ijiɬane wajesesuka beka jaseetijopija umtʰenwa isikʰulu sikakʰandakʰe iŋkosikazi jaseetijopija eɓipʰezu kweŋǀ̤eɓo jajo joŋke eɓifikile ed͡ʒerusalema izakukʰuleka iɓisiɓuja iɬezi eŋǃoleni jajo umprofetʰi uisaja umoja watʰi kufilipʰu sondela unamatʰele kulejo ŋǃola ufilipʰu wajeseɡid͡ʒimela kujo wajizwa umprofetʰi uisaja watʰi ujakuǃonda lokʰu okufundajo jona jatʰi ŋiŋakwazi kaɲd͡ʒani kuŋekʰo oŋiholajo jamŋǁusa ufilipʰu ukuɓa akʰwele aɬale najo kepʰa isaɬukwana eɓisifunda jilesi esitʰi wajiswa ekuɬat͡ʃweni ɲd͡ʒeŋemvu ɲd͡ʒeŋewunɮu elitʰule pʰambi komɡundi kaɲd͡ʒalo kawuvulaŋa wakʰe ekutʰoɓeleni kwakʰe ukwaɬulelwa kwakʰe ŋuɓani oŋalanda iŋkosi jajisitʰi kuje hamba ŋokuɓa ujisit͡ʃa esikʰetʰiwejo sokupʰatʰa iɡama pʰambi kwaɓezizwe namakʰosi naɓantwana ɓakwaisrajeli ŋokuɓa ŋizakumbonisa koŋke ukuɬuʃwa ŋakʰo ŋeŋǁa jeɡama kʰona uananija upetru ukʰona lapʰo ɓatʰuma kuje amaɓili emŋǀeŋa etʰi uŋaliɓali kitʰi wajesesuka upetru naɓo esefikile ɓamjisa elipʰezulu aɓafelokazi ɓoŋke ɓeza kuje ɓekʰala ɓembonisa izambatʰo neziŋuɓo aɓezenzile pʰambi kwaɓo epʰilile kwezwakala lokʰo loŋke id͡ʒopʰa aɓaniŋi ɓakʰolwa jiŋkosi wajeseɬala eziniŋi ed͡ʒopʰa kwasimoni umʃuki kwakukʰona ekesarija etʰile eɡama lajo liŋukorneliju ejinduna jekʰulu jeɓutʰo elitʰiwa elaseitalija wajeŋumuntu okʰolwajo nowesaɓa uŋkuluŋkulu kaɲe nenɮu jakʰe joŋke aɓela aɓantu aɓampofu izipʰo eziniŋi ekʰuleka kuŋkuluŋkulu ɲd͡ʒaloɲd͡ʒalo waɓona ŋokusoɓala iŋelosi kaŋkuluŋkulu iŋena kuje kuŋatʰi ŋehora lesiʃijaɡaloluɲe itʰi korneliju wajiɡǃ̤olozela enokwesaɓa watʰi kwenze ɲd͡ʒani ŋkosi jatʰi kuje imikʰuleko jakʰo nokwaɓela kwakʰo aɓampofu izipʰo kweɲukile kwaɓa jisikʰumbuzo emeɬweni kaŋkuluŋkulu tʰumake ed͡ʒopʰa uɓize usimoni otʰile otʰiwa upetru jena uŋenisile kwasimoni otʰile umʃuki onɮu jakʰe iŋaselwanɮe isimukile iŋelosi eɓikʰuluma naje waɓiza aɓaɓili ɓenɮu jakʰe neɓutʰo elikʰolwajo ajeɬala naje ɲd͡ʒalo waɓalandisa koŋke waɓatʰumela ed͡ʒopʰa ŋaŋomuso ɓesahamba laɓo seɓesondela upetru weɲukela pʰezu kwenɮu ukujokʰuleka ŋehora lesitʰupʰa kʰona kakʰulu ukuɮa kepʰa ɓesamluŋisela weɬelwa jisijezi waɓona nesit͡ʃa esitʰile seɬa siɲd͡ʒeŋendwaŋu eŋkulu seɬiselwa emɬaɓeni ŋamaǀʰopʰo kusona kwakukʰona zoŋke ezineziɲawo nezinwaɓuzelajo zomɬaɓa neziɲoni kwavela latʰi kuje vuka petru ɬaɓa uɮe kepʰa upetru watʰi ǃʰa ŋkosi ŋokuɓa aŋizaŋe ŋikuɮe okujiǀʰilo nokuŋǀ̤olilejo izwi lapʰinda laʃo kuje ŋokwesiɓili latʰi lokʰo akuɬambululile uŋkuluŋkulu uŋaʃo ukutʰi kuɓi lokʰo kwapʰindwa katʰatʰu isit͡ʃa seɲuselwa masiɲane upetru esasambatʰekile ŋokutʰi ŋakuɓe ujini awuɓonilejo beka ajetʰuɲiwe ŋukorneliju eseɓuzile inɮu kasimoni ŋasesaŋweni eɓuza ukutʰi usimoni otʰiwa upetru uŋenisile jini lapʰo upetru esazinɮa ŋombono umoja watʰi kuje beka amaɓili ajakufuna weɬe naɓo uŋaŋaɓazi ŋalutʰo ŋokuɓa jimina eŋiɓatʰumilejo upetru wajeseɬela watʰi bekani jimina enimfunajo kujindaɓani ŋajo ɓatʰi ukorneliju jekʰulu eluŋilejo nemesaɓajo uŋkuluŋkulu kaɬe soŋke saɓad͡ʒuda ujaliwe jiŋelosi eŋǀ̤wele ukuɓa akuɓizele enɮini jakʰe wajeseɓaɓiza waɓaŋenisa ŋaŋomuso naɓo aɓatʰile ɓaɓazalwane ɓased͡ʒopʰa ɓampʰelekezela ŋaŋomuso ɓaŋena ekesarija ukorneliju wajeɓalindele eseɓizile iziɬoɓo naɓaŋane ɓakʰe aɓakʰulu kwatʰi ukuɓa aŋene upetru ukorneliju wamɬaŋaɓeza pʰansi ŋaseziɲaweni zakʰe wakʰuleka kepʰa upetru watʰi sukuma ŋiŋumuntu ɲd͡ʒe esakʰuluma naje waŋena aɓaniŋi aɓaɓeɓutʰene wajesetʰi nijazi ukutʰi akuvuɲelwe ukuɓa oŋumd͡ʒuda aɬaŋane nowesiɲe kepʰa uŋkuluŋkulu uŋit͡ʃeŋisile ukuɓa ŋiŋaʃo naŋojedwa ukutʰi uneǀʰilo nokutʰi uŋǀ̤olile ŋakʰo lokʰu ŋiɓiziwe ŋizile ŋiŋalaŋa ŋakʰoke seŋijaɓuza ukutʰi niŋiɓizeleni ukorneliju watʰi ŋezinsuku eziɮule ŋaleli ɓeŋenza umkʰuleko lesiʃijaɡaloluɲe enɮini jami beka ejembetʰe iŋuɓo ekʰazimulajo jema pʰambi jatʰi ‘korneliju ukukʰuleka kwakʰo nokwaɓela kwakʰo aɓampofu izipʰo kukʰuɲd͡ʒuliwe pʰambi kukaŋkuluŋkulu ŋakʰo tʰumela ed͡ʒopʰa uɓize usimoni otʰiwa upetru jena uŋenisile enɮini kasimoni umʃuki ŋaselwanɮe ŋase ŋitʰumela ŋaso sikʰatʰi kaɬe maɲd͡ʒe sesikʰona soŋke pʰambi kukaŋkuluŋkulu ukuɓa koŋke okujalelwe jiŋkosi kʰona upetru watʰi nembala ŋijaɓona ukutʰi uŋkuluŋkulu akabeki uɓuso ɓamuntu zoŋke omesaɓajo ukuluŋa ujamukeleka kuje walitʰumela kuɓantwana ɓakwaisrajeli eʃumajela ivaŋeli lokutʰula ŋaje ud͡ʒesu kristu jena ujiŋkosi jaɓo ɓoŋke nijalazi elameɲezelwa ed͡ʒudija loŋke liǃalile eɡalile kokubapatʰiza akuʃumajelajo ud͡ʒohane lokutʰi uŋkuluŋkulu wamɡǀ̤oɓa ud͡ʒesu wasenazaretʰa ŋomoja oŋǀ̤wele naŋamanɮa epʰulukisa ɓoŋke aɓaɓesemanɮeni kasatʰane ŋokuɓa uŋkuluŋkulu wajenaje natʰi siŋofakazi ɓezinto zoŋke azenzajo laɓad͡ʒuda nased͡ʒerusalema jena aɓambulalajo ɓempʰaɲeka emtʰini lowo uŋkuluŋkulu ŋosuku lwesitʰatʰu ukuɓa aɓonakale kuŋekuɓantu ɓoŋke kitʰina esiŋofakazi aɓaɓekʰetʰwe ŋuŋkuluŋkulu ŋapʰambili esasiɮa sipʰuza naje kwakʰe kwaɓafilejo wasijala ukuɓa siʃumajele kuɓantu ukutʰi ŋuje ŋuŋkuluŋkulu ukuɓa aɓe ŋumaɬuleli waɓapʰilajo naɓafilejo ŋaje ɓoŋke aɓaprofetʰi ɓafakaza ukutʰi ŋeɡama lakʰe ɓoŋke aɓakʰolwa ŋuje ɓajakwamukela ukutʰetʰelelwa kwatʰi upetru esakʰuluma umoja oŋǀ̤wele weɬela pʰezu kwaɓo ɓoŋke aɓaɓelizwa aɓokusoka aɓakʰolwajo aɓaɓefikile nopetru ɓamaŋala kakʰulu ŋokuɓa isipʰo sikamoja oŋǀ̤wele sitʰeliwe napʰezu kwaɓezizwe ŋokuɓa ɓaɓezwa ɓekʰuluma ŋezilimi ɓetusa uŋkuluŋkulu kʰona upetru wapʰendula watʰi ukʰona jini oŋala ukuɓa ɓaŋabapatʰizwa laɓa aɓamukela umoja oŋǀ̤wele ɲd͡ʒeŋatʰi wajesejala ukuɓa ɓabapatʰizwe eɡameni leŋkosi ɓase ɓemŋǀeŋa ukuɓa aɬale ezitʰile kepʰa aɓapʰostoli naɓazalwane aɓased͡ʒudija ɓezwa ukutʰi naɓezizwe ɓalamukele likaŋkuluŋkulu kwatʰi ukuɓa upetru eɲukele ed͡ʒerusalema aɓokusoka ɓapʰikisana naje ɓatʰi uŋene kuɓantu aɓaŋasokile waɮa naɓo kepʰa upetru waɓatʰatʰela koŋke ŋokulandelana watʰi mina ɓeŋisemzini wased͡ʒopʰa ŋikʰuleka ŋeɬelwa jisijezi ŋaɓona kweɬa isit͡ʃa esitʰile siɲd͡ʒeŋendwaŋu eŋkulu jeɬiswa ŋamaǀʰopʰo jaze jafika kwatʰi ukuɓa ŋijiɡǃ̤olozele ŋabekisisa ŋaɓona zomɬaɓa ezineziɲawo zasenɮe nezinwaɓuzelajo neziɲoni ŋezwa litʰi ‘sukuma petru ɬaɓa uɮe kepʰa ŋatʰi ‘ǃʰa ŋkosi ŋokuɓa okujiǀʰilo nokuŋǀ̤olilejo akuzaŋe kuŋene emloɲeni kʰona lapʰendula ŋokwesiɓili latʰi ‘lokʰo akuɬambululilejo uŋkuluŋkulu uŋaʃo ukutʰi kujiǀʰilo lokʰoke katʰatʰu koŋke kwaɓuje kweɲuselwa bekani ŋaso sikʰatʰi amatʰatʰu pʰambi kwenɮu esasikujo ajetʰuɲelwe ekesarija umoja wajesetʰi aŋihambe naɓo ŋiŋaŋaɓazi ŋalutʰo ɓaŋipʰelekezela laɓo ɓazalwane aɓajisitʰupʰa saja saŋena enɮini jalejo jasiɓikelake ukutʰi jajiɓonile iŋelosi enɮini jajo itʰi ‘tʰumela ed͡ʒopʰa usimoni otʰiwa upetru ozakukʰuluma ŋawo nenɮu jakʰo joŋke ŋatʰi ŋisaǃala ukukʰuluma umoja oŋǀ̤wele weɬela pʰezu kwaɓo ɲd͡ʒeŋakitʰi ekuǃaleni ŋalikʰumbulake leŋkosi ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰo jatʰi ‘ud͡ʒohane wabapatʰiza ŋamanzi nizakubapatʰizwa ŋomoja oŋǀ̤wele ŋakʰo uŋkuluŋkulu eɓanikile ɓona isipʰo ɲd͡ʒeŋatʰi esakʰolwa jiŋkosi ud͡ʒesu kristu ŋiŋuɓani ɓafika efenike nasekʰupro naseantijokija ɓeŋalikʰulumi kojedwa kuɓad͡ʒuda kupʰela kodwa kwakukʰona aɓaɲe kuɓo asekʰupro nasekʰurene aɓatʰi ɓefika eantijokija ɓakʰuluma nakumaɡreki ɓeʃumajela ivaŋeli ŋeŋkosi ud͡ʒesu isanɮa seŋkosi sasinaɓo kwakʰolwa aɓaniŋi kakʰulu ɓapʰendukela eŋkosini kepʰa ŋaɓo ezinɮeɓeni zeɓanɮa lased͡ʒerusalema litʰuma uɓarnaɓa ukuɓa eantijokija watʰi ukuɓa aɓone kaŋkuluŋkulu watʰokoza waɓajala ɓoŋke ukuɓa ɓanamatʰele eŋkosini ŋokuzimisela inɬizijo ŋokuɓa wajejindoda enɬe eɡǀ̤wele umoja oŋǀ̤wele nokukʰolwa eŋkosini aɓantu aɓaniŋi uɓarnaɓa wajeseja etarsu ukuɓa usawulu kwatʰi wamjisa eantijokija kwase ukuɓa umɲaka woŋke ɓaɬaŋane eɓanɮeni ɓefundisa aɓantu aɓaniŋi kwaǃala eantijokija ukuɓa aɓafundi ɓatʰiwe amakristu ŋalezo kweɬela eantijokija aɓaprofetʰi ɓevela ed͡ʒerusalema kwasukuma omuɲe kuɓo oɡama lakʰe liŋuaɡaɓu wakʰomba ŋomoja ukutʰi kuzakuɓa kʰona inɮala loŋke jaɓa kʰona emiɬeni kakxawudiju aɓafundi ɓase ɓezimisela ukuɓa jilowo kuɓo atʰumele umfowaɓo kad͡ʒohane ŋeŋkemba eseɓonile ukutʰi lokʰu kujaɓatʰokozisa aɓad͡ʒuda waǃʰuɓeka nopetru kwakujizinsuku zeziŋkwa eziŋenamvuɓelo wambamba etiloŋweni emavijweni jilelo linamaɓutʰo ukuɓa eɬose kwamaɓutʰo amaɓili eɓoʃiwe ŋamaketaŋa amaɓili naɓalindi pʰambi komɲaŋo ɓeɡǀ̤ina itiloŋo beka jafika iŋelosi jeŋkosi kwakʰaɲa ukukʰaɲa etiloŋweni jamʃaja upetru oɬaŋotʰini jamvusa itʰi ʃeʃa ajesewa amaketaŋa ezanɮeni zakʰe iŋelosi jatʰi kuje ɡǃ̤oka iziǀatʰulo zakʰo wenze ɲd͡ʒalo jatʰi kuje jembatʰa iŋuɓo jakʰo uŋilandele wapʰuma wajilandela wajeŋazi ukutʰi kujiǃiniso jiŋelosi wajetʰi uɓona seɓeɮulile kuɓalindi ɓokuǃala naɓesiɓili ɓafika esaŋweni elija laɓavulekela ŋokwalo ɓapʰuma ɓaɮula saɓa siɲe iŋelosi jajisimʃija masiɲane upetru esesaŋulukile watʰi maɲd͡ʒe seŋijazi ŋeǃiniso ukutʰi iŋkosi itʰumile iŋelosi jajo jaŋikʰulula esanɮeni sikaherode nakukʰo koŋke okubekwe jisizwe saɓad͡ʒuda sekumkʰaɲele lokʰo enɮini kamarija kad͡ʒohane otʰiwa umarku lapʰo ɓeɓeɓutʰene kʰona aɓaniŋi ɓekʰuleka eseŋǃ̤oŋǃ̤otʰa sesaŋo jeza ukusaɓela eɡama lajo liŋuroda likapetru ajivulaŋa esaŋweni ŋeŋǁa jokutʰokoza kepʰa jaɡid͡ʒima jaɓika ukutʰi upetru ŋasesaŋweni kodwa ɓatʰi kujo ujaɬaɲa jona jaǃinisa jatʰi ɦaji kuɲd͡ʒalo ɓona ɓatʰi jiŋelosi jakʰe kepʰa upetru waǃinisa waŋǃ̤oŋǃ̤otʰa seɓevulile ɓaɓona ukutʰi ŋuje ɓamaŋala wajeseɓaǃʰweɓa ŋesanɮa ukuɓa ɓatʰule waɓalandisa ukutʰi iŋkosi imkʰipʰe kaɲd͡ʒani etiloŋweni watʰi ɓikelani ud͡ʒakoɓe naɓazalwane lokʰu wajesepʰuma waja kweɲe sekusile kwaɓa kʰona ukuɲakaza okukʰulu pʰakatʰi kwamaɓutʰo kokutʰi upetru weɬelwe jini uherode jamʃaja kʰona lapʰo ŋokuɓa eŋanikaŋa uŋkuluŋkulu waɮiwa jizimpetʰu kodwa likaŋkuluŋkulu lakʰula kepʰa oɓarnaɓa nosawulu ɓaɓuja ed͡ʒerusalema seɓeǃede ukukʰonza kwaɓo ɓehamba ɓenod͡ʒohane otʰiwa umarku ɓasuka lapʰo ɓaja ekʰupro ŋomkʰumbi ekufikeni kwaɓo esalami ɓaʃumajela likaŋkuluŋkulu emasinaɡoɡeni aɓad͡ʒuda ɓaɓe nod͡ʒohane ejisikʰonzi saɓo seɓedaɓule isiǃʰiŋi soŋke ɓaze ɓafika epʰafu ɓafumana
