ŋokuhuɲuʃwa naɓo ukupʰambukisa ekukʰolweni kepʰa usawulu osetʰiwa upawulu eɡǀ̤wele umoja oŋǀ̤wele wamɡǃ̤olozela watʰi o oɡǀ̤wele iŋkoɬiso joŋke noɓuɓi ɓoŋke kasatʰane sitʰa sokuluŋa koŋke awujikujeka ukuzipʰambukisa izinɮela eziǃondilejo zeŋkosi beka isanɮa seŋkosi sipʰezu kwakʰo maɲd͡ʒe uzakuɓa jimpumputʰe kuɓe jisikʰatʰi uŋaliɓoni ilaŋa kwase kʰona lapʰo ukufipʰala noɓumɲama aɓazakumhola ŋesanɮa kʰona eseɓona okwenzekilejo wakʰolwa emaŋaliswa ŋesifundiso seŋkosi upawulu naɓaɓe naje ɓamuka epʰafu ŋomkʰumbi ɓafika epʰerɡe lasepʰamfilija kepʰa ud͡ʒohane waɬukana naɓo waɓujela ed͡ʒerusalema ɓona kwaɓo epʰerɡe ɓaja eantijokija lasepʰisidija ɓaŋena esinaɡoɡeni ŋosuku lwesaɓatʰa ɓaɬala pʰansi sekufundiwe umtʰetʰo naɓaprofetʰi aɓapʰatʰi ɓesinaɡoɡe ɓatʰumela kuɓo ɓatʰi madoda ɓazalwane lokujala aɓantu kʰulumani wajesesukuma upawulu waǃʰweɓa ŋesanɮa watʰi madoda akwaisrajeli enesaɓa uŋkuluŋkulu uŋkuluŋkulu sakwaisrajeli waɓakʰetʰa oɓaɓa waɓapʰakamisa aɓantu ɓeŋaɓafokazi laseɡiɓitʰe waɓakʰipʰa ŋeŋalo epʰakemejo waɓaɓekezelela eɬane kuŋatʰi imiɲaka eŋamaʃumi waǀʰitʰa ezijisikʰombisa lasekʰanani waɓaɓela liɓe jifa kwaɮula kuŋatʰi imiɲaka eŋamakʰulu namaʃumi ajisiɬanu emva kwalokʰo waɓanika aɓaɬuleli kwaɓa ŋusamuweli umprofetʰi kusukela lapʰo ɓaǀela iŋkosi uŋkuluŋkulu waɓanika usawule kakisi sakwaɓeɲd͡ʒamini imiɲaka eŋamaʃumi esemkʰipʰile waɓavusela udavide aɓe jiŋkosi ŋaje ukutʰi ‘ŋimfumene udavide kad͡ʒesaji oŋowenɬizijo jami ojakwenza koŋke eŋikutʰandajo enzalweni jakʰe uŋkuluŋkulu waletʰela uisrajeli umsindisi ud͡ʒesu ɲd͡ʒeŋokwetʰembisa kwakʰe eŋakafiki jena ud͡ʒohane wajeseʃumajele soŋke sakwaisrajeli umbhapatʰizo wokupʰenduka eseɡǀ̤ina kwakʰe ud͡ʒohane watʰi ‘lokʰu enitʰi ŋijikʰo aŋisikʰo kodwa bekani ujeza eŋiŋafanele ukukʰumula isiǀatʰulo seziɲawo zakʰe madoda ɓazalwane oɬaŋa lukaaɓrahama naɓapʰakatʰi aɓamesaɓajo uŋkuluŋkulu litʰuɲelwe kitʰi ŋokuɓa aɓakʰilejo ed͡ʒerusalema naɓaɓusi ɓaɓo aɓamazaŋa jena aɓaprofetʰi amasaɓatʰa ŋamasaɓatʰa ɓawaɡǀ̤walisa ŋokumlaɬa nakuɓa ɓeŋafumanaŋa iǀala kuje nokʰo ɓaǀela kupilatu ukuɓa aɓulawe kwatʰi seɓefeze koŋke okwakulot͡ʃiwe ŋaje ɓameɬisa emtʰini ɓambeka etʰuneni kepʰa uŋkuluŋkulu kwaɓafilejo waɓonwa eziniŋi jiɓo aɓaɓekʰupʰukele naje ed͡ʒerusalema ɓevela eɡalile aseɓeŋofakazi ɓakʰe kuɓantu maɲd͡ʒe natʰi siniʃumajeza ivaŋeli lesitʰembiso koɓaɓa ukutʰi uŋkuluŋkulu usiɡǀ̤walisile kuɓantwana ɓetʰu ŋokumvusa ud͡ʒesu ɲd͡ʒeŋokuɓa kulot͡ʃiwe futʰi ihuɓo lesiɓili ukutʰi ‘wena ujindodana jami namuɬa ŋikuzele maǃondana kwakʰe kwaɓafilejo ukuɓa eŋasajikuɓujela ekuɓoleni wakʰuluma kaɲd͡ʒe watʰi ‘ŋizakuninika okuŋǀ̤wele nokutʰembekilejo kukadavide ŋakʰo nakweɲe utʰi ‘awujikunika oŋǀ̤wele wakʰo aɓone ukuɓola ŋokuɓa udavide esekʰonzile iǀeɓo likaŋkuluŋkulu sakʰe uɓutʰoŋo waɓekwa kojise waɓona ukuɓola kepʰa jena amvusajo uŋkuluŋkulu akakuɓonaŋa ukuɓola ŋakʰoke ɓazalwane ukutʰi ŋalowo kumeɲezelwa ukutʰetʰelelwa nakukʰo koŋke eɓeniŋenakuluŋisiswa kukʰo ŋomtʰetʰo kamose jilowo okʰolwajo ujakuluŋisiswa ŋaje ŋakʰo ǃapʰelani neɬelwe ŋokwakʰuluɲwa ŋaɓaprofetʰi ukutʰi ‘bekani nimaŋale niɲamalale ŋokuɓa ŋiseɓenza umseɓenzi emiɬeni jenu umseɓenzi eniŋajikukʰolwa jiwo nakuɓa ŋawo kwatʰi ekupʰumeni kwaɓo ɓaɓaǀela ukuɓa akʰuluɲwe kuɓo naŋesaɓatʰa elizajo kʰona seɓeɬakazekile aɓesinaɡoɡe aɓaniŋi ɓaɓad͡ʒuda aǃotʰo ɓalandela opawulu noɓarnaɓa aɓakʰuluma naɓo ɓeɓaŋǀeŋa ukuɓa ɓaɬale kaŋkuluŋkulu ŋesaɓatʰa elilandelajo kwaɓutʰana kuǀiʃe woŋke likaŋkuluŋkulu kepʰa aɓad͡ʒuda ɓeɓona iziǁuku ɓaɡǀ̤wala ɓakupʰika okwakukʰuluɲwa ŋupawulu ɓeɬambalaza kʰona opawulu noɓarnaɓa ɓakʰuluma ŋesiɓindi ɓatʰi ɓekudiŋeka ukuɓa likaŋkuluŋkulu likʰuluɲwe kuǃala kepʰa lokʰu niliŋǃaɓa niziʃo nitʰi ukupʰila okupʰakade bekani sesipʰendukela kwaɓezizwe ŋokuɓa iŋkosi isijalezile kaɲd͡ʒalo ukutʰi ‘ŋikuɓekile uɓe ŋukukʰaɲa kwaɓezizwe uɓe jinsindiso kuɓe semkʰawulweni womɬaɓa kwatʰi aɓezizwe ɓekuzwa lokʰo ɓatʰokoza ɓalidumisa leŋkosi ɓakʰolwa ɓoŋke aɓaɓemiselwe ukupʰila okupʰakade izwi leŋkosi lahaɲd͡ʒiswa loŋke kepʰa aɓad͡ʒuda ɓavusa aɓesifazane aɓaǃotʰo aɓanesitʰunzi nezikʰulu ɓavusela opawulu noɓarnaɓa ukuziŋelwa ɓaɓaǁoʃa emikʰawulweni jaɓo ɓonake ɓaɓavutʰululela utʰuli lweziɲawo zaɓo ɓeza eikoniju aɓafundi ɓaɡǀ̤wala nomoja oŋǀ̤wele kwatʰi eikoniju ɓaŋena kaɲekaɲe esinaɡoɡeni laɓad͡ʒuda ɓakʰuluma kwakʰolwa isiǁuku esikʰulu saɓad͡ʒuda namaɡreki kepʰa aɓad͡ʒuda aɓaŋakʰolwaŋa ɓavusa aɓezizwe ɓaɓenza nɬizijombi ŋakuɓazalwane nokʰo ɓaɬala isikʰatʰi ɓefundisa ŋesiɓindi ŋeŋkosi ejafakazela wajo iɓanika ukuɓa iziɓonakaliso nezimaŋaliso ŋezanɮa zaɓo kepʰa isiǁuku saɬukana pʰakatʰi aɓaɲe ɓaɓa ŋakuɓad͡ʒuda naɓaɲe ŋakuɓapʰostoli kwatʰi ukuɓa ɓasukelwe jisidumo saɓezizwe naɓad͡ʒuda kaɲe naɓaɓusi ɓaɓo sokuɓapʰatʰa kaɓi nokuɓakʰanda ŋamat͡ʃe ɓatʰi seɓekwazi lokʰo ɓaɓalekela jaselikawonija ilistra nederɓe laŋakʰona ɓaʃumajela kʰona ivaŋeli elistra kwakuɬezi etʰile ejisilima ŋeziɲawo ejisiʃoʃa selokʰu jazalwa ŋunina eŋazaŋe jona jamuzwa upawulu ekʰuluma jena ejiɡǃ̤olozela waɓona ukutʰi inokukʰolwa kokuɓa ipʰiliswe watʰi ŋezwi elikʰulu sukuma ŋeziɲawo zakʰo jajisiɡǁ̤uma jahamba kwatʰike iziǁuku zikuɓona lokʰo upawulu zapʰakamisa zatʰi ŋesilikawonija oŋkuluŋkulu ɓefana naɓantu ɓeɬele kitʰi uɓarnaɓa ɓambiza ŋokutʰi ud͡ʒupitʰeri upawulu ŋokutʰi umerkuriju ŋokuɓa kwakuŋuje owajehola ekukʰulumeni kepʰa kad͡ʒupitʰeri otʰempeli lakʰe lipʰambi waletʰa iziŋkunzi nemiɡeǁo jezimbali ŋasemasaŋweni ukuɓaɬaɓela ekaɲe neziǁuku kwatʰi ukuɓa ɓakuzwe lokʰo aɓapʰostoli oɓarnaɓa nopawulu ɓakxebula iziŋuɓo zaɓo ɓapʰonseka pʰakatʰi kwesiǁuku ɓememeza ɓetʰi madoda lokʰu natʰi siŋaɓantu aɓaɲd͡ʒeŋani ŋemvelo siniʃumajeza ivaŋeli ukuɓa nipʰenduke kulokʰo okujize nipʰendukele kuŋkuluŋkulu opʰilajo nomɬaɓa nolwanɮe nakʰo koŋke okukukʰo otʰe ŋezizukulwane eziɮulilejo wajeka zoŋke ŋezinɮela nokʰo akajekaŋa ŋokwenza okuɬe jasezulwini nezikʰatʰi eɡǀ̤walisa izinɬizijo ŋokuɬe naŋokud͡ʒaɓula ɓekuʃo lokʰo ɓazijekisa kalukʰuni iziǁuku ukuɓa ziŋaɓaɬaɓeli kodwa aɓad͡ʒuda ɓevela eantijokija naseikoniju seɓezivumisile iziǁuku ɓamkʰanda upawulu ŋamat͡ʃe ɓamhudulela ŋapʰanɮe ɓetʰi kepʰa kwatʰi aɓafundi ɓembuŋaɲele waŋena ŋaŋomuso noɓarnaɓa ɓaja ederɓe seɓeliʃumajele ivaŋeli ɓezuzile aɓafundi aɓaniŋi ɓaɓujela elistra naseikoniju naseantijokija ɓaǃinisa imipʰefumulo jaɓafundi ɓeɓaluleka ukuɓa ɓeme ekukʰolweni ɓetʰi simelwe ukuŋena kaŋkuluŋkulu ŋezinɬupʰeko eziniŋi seɓeɓakʰetʰele amaluŋa amaɓanɮa ŋamaɓanɮa ɓakʰuleka ɓezila ukuɮa ɓaɓanikela eŋkosini aseɓekʰolwa jijo ɓase ɓedaɓula ipʰisidija ɓaja epʰamfilija seɓekʰulumile epʰerɡe ɓeɬela eatalija ɓasuka lapʰo ŋomkʰumbi ɓaja eantijokija lapʰo ɓaɓenikelwe kʰona kaŋkuluŋkulu mseɓenzi aseɓewufezile kwatʰi ukuɓa ɓafike ɓaliɓutʰa iɓanɮa ɓalanda ŋakʰo koŋke uŋkuluŋkulu ŋaɓo nokutʰi naɓezizwe isaŋo lokukʰolwa ɓase ɓeɬala naɓafundi isikʰatʰi esiŋesiŋǀane kweɬa aɓatʰile ed͡ʒudija ɓafundisa aɓazalwane ukutʰi uma niŋasokwa ŋomtʰetʰo kamose niŋesindiswe kutʰe ukuɓa ukupʰambana nokupʰikisana okukʰulu pʰakatʰi kwaɓo nopawulu noɓarnaɓa ɓaŋǃuma ukuɓa opawulu noɓarnaɓa naɓatʰile kuɓo ɓakʰupʰukele ed͡ʒerusalema kuɓapʰostoli namaluŋa ŋalejo ndaɓa ŋalokʰo ɓepʰelekezelwe jiɓanɮa ɓadaɓula ifenike nesamarija ɓalandisa ukupʰenduka kwaɓezizwe ɓenzela ɓoŋke aɓazalwane eŋkulu seɓefikile ed͡ʒerusalema ɓamukelwa jiɓanɮa naɓapʰostoli namaluŋa ɓakuɓika koŋke uŋkuluŋkulu aɓekwenzile ŋaɓo kepʰa aɓatʰile ɓeɬelo laɓafarisi aɓakʰolwajo ɓatʰi ukuɓa ɓasokwe ɓajalwe ukuɡǀ̤ina umtʰetʰo kamose ɓase ɓeɓutʰana aɓapʰostoli namaluŋa ɓajiɬole lejo ndaɓa seɓepʰikisene kakʰulu upetru watʰi kuɓo madoda ɓazalwane nijazi ukutʰi uŋkuluŋkulu wakʰetʰa pʰakatʰi ukuɓa aɓezizwe ɓezwe levaŋeli ŋomlomo ɓakʰolwe uŋkuluŋkulu inɬizijo waɓafakazela eɓapʰa umoja oŋǀ̤wele ɲd͡ʒeŋatʰi futʰi akaɬukanisaŋa ŋalutʰo pʰakatʰi kwetʰu naɓo eɬambulula izinɬizijo zaɓo ŋokukʰolwa maɲd͡ʒeke nimliŋelani uŋkuluŋkulu ŋokuɓeka id͡ʒoka entaɲeni jaɓafundi oɓaɓa natʰi esasiŋenamanɮa okulitʰwala kepʰa sijakʰolwa ukutʰi ŋomusa weŋkosi ud͡ʒesu ŋanɮelaɲe naɓo isiǁuku soŋke satʰula ɓaɓelalela oɓarnaɓa nopawulu ɓelanda ŋeziɓonakaliso naŋezimaŋaliso zoŋke uŋkuluŋkulu aɓezenzile ŋaɓo pʰakatʰi kwaɓezizwe kepʰa seɓetʰulile ud͡ʒakoɓe watʰatʰa watʰi madoda ɓazalwane ŋilaleleni usimejoni ŋokuɬela kukaŋkuluŋkulu ekuǃaleni ukuɓa atʰatʰele iɡama lakʰe kuɓo aɓezizwe namazwi aɓaprofetʰi ajavumelana nalokʰo ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰo kulot͡ʃiwe ukutʰi ‘emva kwalokʰo ŋijakuɓuja ŋijakʰe futʰi inɮu kadavide ewilejo ŋiɓuje ŋakʰe okudilikilejo kwajo ŋijimise aɓaselejo ɓaɓantu kaɲe naɓezizwe ɓoŋke ɓajifune iŋkosi eliɓizwe pʰezu kwaɓo iɡama iʃo iŋkosi lokʰu kwapʰakade ŋakʰo ŋitʰi masiŋaɓakʰatʰazi laɓo kwaɓezizwe aɓapʰendukela kuŋkuluŋkulu masiɓaloɓele ukuɓa ɓajeke amaɲala ezitʰombe nawoɓufeɓe nawokuǃumbelenejo naweɡazi ŋokuɓa umose unaɓo aɓaʃumajelajo joŋke emasinaɡoɡeni amasaɓatʰa ŋamasaɓatʰa kʰona kwaɓa kuɬe kuɓapʰostoli namaluŋa iɓanɮa loŋke ukutʰumela eantijokija nopawulu noɓarnaɓa akʰetʰiwejo pʰakatʰi kwaɓo ud͡ʒuda otʰiwa uɓarsaɓa nosila aŋaɓaholi pʰakatʰi kwaɓazalwane ɓaloɓa ŋesanɮa saɓo ŋokutʰi aɓapʰostoli namaluŋa aɓazalwane ɓajaɓiŋelela aɓazalwane aɓavela kwaɓezizwe aɓaseantijokija naɓasesirija naɓasekʰilikʰija ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰo ukutʰi aɓaɲe aɓavela kitʰi ɓanikʰatʰazile ŋamazwi ɓeɲakazisa imipʰefumulo esiŋaɓajalelaŋa kʰona kwaɓa kuɬe kitʰi sesinɬizijoɲe ukutʰuma akʰetʰiwejo kaɲe naɓatʰandiwejo ɓetʰu oɓarnaɓa nopawulu aɓantu aɓadele ukupʰila kwaɓo ŋeŋǁa jeɡama leŋkosi jetʰu ud͡ʒesu kristu ŋalokʰo sitʰumile od͡ʒuda nosila aɓazakunit͡ʃela ŋomlomo ŋokuɓa kwaɓa kuɬe kumoja oŋǀ̤wele nakitʰi ukuɓa siŋanitʰwesi umtʰwalo omkʰulu ŋapʰanɮe ezifunekajo zokutʰi nijeke okuɬat͡ʃelwe izitʰombe neɡazi nokuǃumbelenejo noɓufeɓe noɓa kaɬe salani kaɬe ŋakʰo seɓemukisiwe ɓeɬela eantijokija ɓaliɓutʰa iɓanɮa ɓalinika iŋǀwadi seɓejifundile ɓatʰokoza ŋenduduzo jajo od͡ʒuda nosila ɲd͡ʒeŋokuɓa naɓo ɓeŋaɓaprofetʰi ɓaɓaduduza aɓazalwane ŋamazwi amaniŋi ɓaɓaǃinisa seɓeɬale kʰona isikʰatʰi ɓamukiswa ŋaɓazalwane ŋokutʰula ɓaɓujela kuɓo aɓaɓatʰumilejo kepʰa kwaɓa kuɬe kusila ukuɓa kʰona kodwa opawulu noɓarnaɓa ɓaɬala eantijokija ɓefundisa ɓeʃumajela leŋkosi kaɲe naɓaɲe aɓaniŋi emva ezitʰile upawulu wajesetʰi kuɓarnaɓa ake siɓuje aɓazalwane joŋke ŋamiɲe esaʃumajela kujo leŋkosi siɓone ukutʰi ɓaɬezi kaɲd͡ʒani uɓarnaɓa waɬosa nod͡ʒohane otʰiwa umarku kepʰa upawulu watʰi ukuɓa ɓahambe naje owaɓaʃija epʰamfilija aja naɓo emseɓenzini kwase ukupʰikisana okukʰulu ɓaze ɓaɬukana uɓarnaɓa watʰatʰa umarku ekʰupro ŋomkʰumbi kepʰa upawulu wazikʰetʰela usila ŋaɓazalwane weŋkosi wadaɓula isirija nekʰilikʰija eǃinisa amaɓanɮa kʰona weɬela ederɓe naselistra beka kwakukʰona lapʰo otʰile ŋutʰimotʰewu iɡama lakʰe jowesifazane wakwad͡ʒuda okʰoliwejo kepʰa ujise wajeŋumɡreki owajefakazelwa kaɬe ŋaɓazalwane ɓaselistra naɓaseikoniju lowo upawulu watʰanda ukuɓa naje wamtʰatʰa ŋeŋǁa jaɓad͡ʒuda aɓaɓekʰona ŋokuɓa ɓoŋke ɓaɓemazi ukutʰi ujise wajeŋumɡreki kwatʰi ɓedaɓula ɓaɓanika iziŋǃumo ezaŋǃuɲwa ŋaɓapʰostoli namaluŋa ased͡ʒerusalema ukuɓa ɓaziɡǀ̤ine ɲd͡ʒaloke amaɓanɮa aǃiniswa ekukʰolweni ŋoɓuniŋi imiɬa ŋemiɬa ɓase ɓedaɓula lasefriɡija nelaseɡalatʰija ɓeŋǃat͡ʃelwe ŋumoja oŋǀ̤wele ukulikʰuluma easija seɓefikile ŋasemisija ɓaliŋa ukuja eɓitʰinija kepʰa umoja kad͡ʒesu akaɓavumelaŋa ɓaɮula emisija ɓeɬela etrowa kwaɓonakala kupawulu eɓusuku etʰile jasemakedonija ejajimi imŋǀeŋa jatʰi welela emakedonija lapʰo esewuɓonile masiɲane ukuja emakedonija satʰi uŋkuluŋkulu usiɓizile ukuɓa siɓaʃumajeze ivaŋeli kʰona etrowa ŋomkʰumbi saǃonda esamotrake ŋaŋomuso enejapʰoli sisuka lapʰo saja efilipi eliŋumuzi ojikʰanda sasemakedonija kulowo saɬala ezitʰile ŋosuku lwesaɓatʰa sapʰumela ŋapʰanɮe kwesaŋo ŋasemfuleni lapʰo satʰi ɓaɓevama ukukʰuleka kʰona saɬala pʰansi sakʰuluma kuɓo aɓesifazane aɓaɓeɓutʰene owesifazane otʰile oɡama lakʰe liŋulidija eŋumtʰeŋisi weziɓuɓende wasetʰijatʰira okʰonza uŋkuluŋkulu iŋkosi jajivula inɬizijo jakʰe ukuɓa aǃapʰele okwakʰuluɲwa ŋupawulu kutʰe esebapatʰiziwe kaɲe nenɮu jakʰe wasiŋǀeŋa watʰi uma nitʰi ŋikʰolekile eŋkosini ŋenani enɮini jami niɬale kʰona wasiǀindezela kwatʰi sija jokukʰuleka kwaɬaŋana natʰi enomoja woɓuŋoma ejajitʰolela aɓaninijo eŋkulu ŋokubula jona jamlandela upawulu natʰi jamemeza jatʰi laɓa ɓantu ɓajiziŋǀeku zikaŋkuluŋkulu opʰezukoŋke inɮela jensindiso jakwenza lokʰo eziniŋi kepʰa upawulu eseǀasukile wapʰenduka watʰi kumoja ŋijakujala eɡameni likad͡ʒesu kristu ukuɓa upʰume kujo wajesepʰuma ŋaso sikʰatʰi kwatʰi aɓaninijo seɓeɓonile ukutʰi itʰemba jaɓo ɓaɓaɓamba opawulu nosila ɓaɓahudulela esiɡǀ̤awini pʰambi kwaɓaɓusi ɓaɓajisa ɓatʰi laɓa ɓantu ɓaɲakazisa wakitʰi ɓeŋaɓad͡ʒuda ɓafundisa imikʰuɓa esiŋavuɲelwe ukuɓa sijamukele sijenze tʰina esiŋamaroma isiǁuku siɓavukela zajala ukuɓa ɓaɬut͡ʃulwe iziŋuɓo ɓaʃajwe ŋenduku seziɓaʃajile eminiŋi zaɓapʰonsa etiloŋweni zajala umɡǀ̤iniziɓoʃwa ukuɓa aɓaɡǀ̤ine jena ejaliwe kaɲd͡ʒalo waɓapʰonsa etiloŋweni eliŋapʰakatʰi waɓopʰa iziɲawo zaɓo oɡoŋolweni kepʰa pʰakatʰi koɓusuku opawulu nosila ɓekʰuleka ɓamdumisa uŋkuluŋkulu ŋamahuɓo iziɓoʃwa zaɓezwa ŋokuzuma komɬaɓa okukʰulu kwazaɲazaɲiswa zetiloŋo kʰona lapʰo imiɲaŋo joŋke kwatʰukuluka neziɓopʰo zaɓo ɓoŋke kwatʰi umɡǀ̤iniziɓoʃwa epʰapʰama waɓona imiɲaŋo jetiloŋo wajesehoʃa iŋkemba ukuziɓulala ŋokuɓa watʰi iziɓoʃwa zipʰuɲukile kepʰa upawulu ŋezwi elikʰulu watʰi uŋazilimazi ŋokuɓa sikʰona soŋke wajeseɓiza iziɓani waɡid͡ʒimela pʰakatʰi etʰutʰumela pʰansi pʰambi kukapawulu nosila waɓakʰipʰela ŋapʰanɮe watʰi makʰosi ŋimelwe ukuɓa ŋisindiswe ɓona ɓatʰi kʰolwa jiŋkosi ud͡ʒesu jikʰona nenɮu jakʰo ɓase ɓemʃumajeza likaŋkuluŋkulu jena naɓo ɓoŋke aɓaɓesenɮini jakʰe waɓatʰatʰa ŋaso sikʰatʰi saseɓusuku waɓaɡeza wabapatʰizwa kʰona lapʰo jena naɓo ɓoŋke aɓakʰe waɓeɲusela enɮini waɓaɓekela ukuɮa watʰokoza kaɲe nenɮu jakʰe joŋke ŋokukʰolwa ŋuŋkuluŋkulu kepʰa zatʰuma izikʰonzi zatʰi ɓakʰulule laɓo ɓantu umɡǀ̤iniziɓoʃwa waɓikela upawulu watʰi izinduna zitʰumele ukuɓa nikʰululwe ŋakʰo pʰumani maɲd͡ʒe ŋokutʰula kepʰa upawulu watʰi ɓasiʃajile pʰambi kwaɓantu siŋalaɬwaŋa ǀala tʰina siŋaɓantu aɓaŋamaroma ɓasipʰonsa etiloŋweni maɲd͡ʒe ɓasikʰipʰa ŋasese ǃʰaɓo ɓona ɓasikʰipʰe izikʰonzi zaɓikela zona zesaɓa ukutʰi ɓaŋamaroma zaɓaŋǀeŋa seziɓakʰipʰile zaɓaŋǁusa ukuɓa ɓamuke ɓase ɓepʰuma etiloŋweni ɓaŋena kwalidija kwatʰi seɓeɓaɓonile aɓazalwane ɓaɓaduduza ɓamuka kwatʰi seɓedaɓulile iamfipʰoli neapʰolonija ɓafika etʰesalonika lapʰo kwakukʰona isinaɡoɡe laɓad͡ʒuda kepʰa upawulu ɲd͡ʒeŋokwenza kwakʰe waŋena kuɓo wapʰendulana naɓo amasaɓatʰa amatʰatʰu etʰatʰela emibalweni eɓavulela eɓaǀʰasisela ukutʰi ukuɓa ukristu aɬupʰeke kwaɓafilejo etʰi futʰi ud͡ʒesu eŋimʃumajela uŋukristu ɓase ɓevuma aɓaɲe kuɓo ɓaziɬaŋanisa nopawulu nosila futʰi nesiǁuku esikʰulu samaɡreki akʰolwajo kaɲe naɓesifazane aɓadumilejo aɓaŋejiŋǀ̤osana kepʰa aɓad͡ʒuda ɓenomhawu ɓatʰatʰa kumabukudwane aɓalisa aɓatʰile aɓaɓi ɓesusa isijalujalu pʰakatʰi kwaɓantu ɓaǁokozelisa ɓaɬasela inɮu kad͡ʒasoni ɓefuna ukuɓakʰipʰela kuɓantu kepʰa ɓeŋaɓafumani ɓamhudulela ud͡ʒasoni kaɲe naɓazalwane aɓatʰile kuɓapʰatʰimuzi ɓamemeza ɓatʰi laɓa aɓajaluzisa loŋke seɓefikile nalapʰa ud͡ʒasoni uɓamukele ɓoŋke laɓa ɓenza okupʰambene zikakesari ɓetʰi kukʰona eɲe iŋkosi ŋud͡ʒesu kepʰa ɓetʰusa isiǁuku naɓapʰatʰimuzi aɓezwa lokʰo ɓatʰatʰa isiɓambiso kud͡ʒasoni nakwaɓaɲe ɓaɓakʰulula kepʰa aɓazalwane ɓamukisa opawulu nosila masiɲane eɓusuku ukuɓa ɓaje eɓereja ɓona seɓefikile kʰona ɓaŋena esinaɡoɡeni laɓad͡ʒuda laɓoke ɓaɓeɓaɬe kunaɓasetʰesalonika ɓalamukela ŋenɬizijo joŋke ɓaɬolisisa imibalo imiɬa ŋemiɬa ukuɓa ziɲd͡ʒalo jini ŋakʰo aɓaniŋi kuɓo ɓakʰolwa naɓesifazane aɓanesitʰunzi aɓaŋamaɡreki aŋejiŋǀ̤osana kwatʰi aɓad͡ʒuda ɓasetʰesalonika seɓezwile ukutʰi likaŋkuluŋkulu limeɲezelwe ŋupawulu naseɓereja ɓeza nakʰona ɓaziɲakazisa ɓezivusa iziǁuku kʰona aɓazalwane ɓamukisa masiɲane upawulu ukuɓa elwanɮe kepʰa osila notʰimotʰewu ɓasala kʰona aɓampʰelekezelajo upawulu ɓamfikisa eatʰene kwatʰi seɓamukele isijalezo ŋosila naŋotʰimotʰewu sokuɓa ɓeze kuje ŋokuʃeʃa okukʰulu ɓamuka kwatʰi upawulu esaɓalinda eatʰene umoja wakʰe waǀunuka pʰakatʰi kwakʰe eɓona uɡǀ̤wele izitʰombe ŋakʰoke wakʰuluma esinaɡoɡeni kuɓad͡ʒuda amakʰolwa nasesiɡǀ̤awini imiɬa ŋemiɬa kuɓo aɓaɓesuke ɓekʰona kepʰa aɓatʰile zamaepikʰuru nezamastojiku ɓapʰikisana naje aɓaɲe ɓatʰi leli pʰoʃopʰoʃo litʰini aɓaɲe ɓatʰi kuŋatʰi uŋomemezela oŋkuluŋkulu aɓaŋaziwajo ŋokuɓa wajeʃumajela ivaŋeli ŋod͡ʒesu naŋokuvuka kwaɓafilejo ɓase ɓemtʰatʰa ɓamjisa earejopʰaɡu ɓetʰi uŋesazise ukutʰi sijini esiʃa esikʰuluɲwa ŋuwe ŋokuɓa uletʰa ezinɮeɓeni zetʰu okutʰile okuŋaziwajo ŋalokʰo ukutʰi lokʰu kuŋaɓa jini
